<h2>코퍼스 — 000/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>000/01_corpus_navigation_map.md</code></h3>
<h1>Corpus Navigation Map</h1>
<p>This repository is a comparative research corpus for coding agents and harnesses. Use this map to decide where to read first without physically moving existing data.</p>
<p>For reversible old-to-new bucket proposals, see <code>000/02_corpus_move_candidates.md</code>.</p>
<p>For the canonical relationship between <code>000/</code> and <code>000_overview/</code>, see <code>000/03_overview_canonical_map.md</code>.</p>

<h3><code>000/03_overview_canonical_map.md</code></h3>
<h1>Overview Canonical Map</h1>
<p>This map resolves the apparent duplication between <code>000/</code> and <code>000_overview/</code> without deleting or moving files.</p>
<h2>Canonical Rule</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>000/</code> is the root overview index and short-entry reading spine.</li>
<li><code>000_overview/</code> is the deep overview source set.</li>
<li>If the same filename exists in both folders and content differs, keep both:
<ul>
<li>read <code>000/&#x3C;name></code> first for orientation,</li>
<li>read <code>000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> for detailed analysis.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>If content is identical, treat <code>000/&#x3C;name></code> as the navigation copy and <code>000_overview/&#x3C;name></code> as the deep-overview location until a later link audit decides whether deduplication is safe.</li>
</ul>

5:["$","$L27","01-corpus-spine",{"id":"01-corpus-spine","order":1,"tier":"developer","title":"코퍼스 읽기 지도 (000)","description":"navigation + canonical map","lang":"ko","children":["$","div",null,{"dangerouslySetInnerHTML":{"__html":"$28"}}]}]
29:T8b2,<h2>한 문장으로 말하면</h2>
<p>Superpowers는 독립적으로 구동되는 별개의 프로그램이 아니라, 기존에 쓰던 코딩 에이전트(Claude Code, Codex 등)에 탑재하여 에이전트가 완벽한 기획과 테스트 중심의 협업을 수행하게 제어하는 개발 방법론 플러그인 세트예요.</p>
<h2>비유로 이해하기</h2>
<p>충동적으로 일단 무작정 벽돌부터 쌓기 시작하는 서툰 인부(기본 AI)에게 "구체적인 건축 설계도를 먼저 그리고, 승인을 받은 뒤, 매 단계마다 수평계와 안전 진단(테스트 코드)을 통과해야만 벽돌을 올리게 가르치는 엄격한 현장 감독 규정"을 장착해 주는 형태예요. 이 규정을 장착하면 에이전트의 뇌가 안전하고 체계적으로 작동해요.</p>
<h2>이런 걸 할 수 있어요</h2>
<ul>
<li>개발을 부탁했을 때 마음대로 코딩하지 않고 질문을 던져 세부 기획 문서를 먼저 작성하도록 유도해요.</li>
<li>기획서가 승인되면 2~5분 단위의 작은 태스크(작업 단위)로 기획서를 알아서 쪼개어 작업해요.</li>
<li>임의 코딩을 금지하고 반드시 실패하는 테스트를 먼저 짠 뒤 코드를 완성하게 통제(TDD 규칙)해요.</li>
<li>서브 에이전트(보조 역할을 하는 가상 에이전트)를 병렬로 호출해서 코드 품질 리뷰와 개발을 나누어 실행하게 해요.</li>
</ul>
<h2>왜 좋냐면요</h2>
<p>기본 코딩 AI는 맥락이 길어질수록 설계 방향성을 잃고 방황하지만, Superpowers 규정을 장착한 에이전트는 계획서의 체크박스를 하나씩 정밀 타격하듯 해치워요. 사람이 세밀하게 모니터링하지 않아도 최장 수 시간 동안 실수 없이 안전하게 개발 업무를 이어가서 개발자의 정신적 피로도를 획기적으로 덜어줘요.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>규정에 묶인 테스트 주도 개발 패턴이나 내부 하위 에이전트 병렬 호출의 기술적 설계 규칙이 궁금하시면 상단 메뉴의 <strong>개발자 문서</strong>를 읽어보세요. 좀 더 고난도의 시스템 규칙들을 깊숙이 파헤치실 수 있어요.</p>
</blockquote>
6:["$","$L27","02-what-is-superpowers",{"id":"02-what-is-superpowers","order":2,"tier":"core","title":"Superpowers가 뭐예요?","description":"한 문장 정의와 비유로 이해하기","lang":"ko","children":["$","div",null,{"dangerouslySetInnerHTML":{"__html":"$29"}}]}]
2a:Taf1,<h2>내 에이전트에 날개 달아주기</h2>
<p>Superpowers는 내가 평소 애용하는 도구에 맞춰 장착해 주면 돼요. 자주 쓰이는 에이전트별 설치 방안을 일목요연하게 알려 드릴게요.</p>
<h3>Claude Code</h3>
<p>클로드 공식 마켓플레이스(플러그인 상점)에서 간편하게 플러그인을 주입해 보세요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">/plugin install superpowers@claude-plugins-official
</code></pre>
<p>또는 공식 마켓 외에 전용 장터를 등록해 설치할 수도 있어요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">/plugin marketplace add obra/superpowers-marketplace
/plugin install superpowers@superpowers-marketplace
</code></pre>
<h3>Codex CLI</h3>
<p>Codex 콘솔 화면에서 플러그인 리스트를 열어서 활성화해 주세요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">/plugins
</code></pre>
<p>목록이나 검색 창에 <code>superpowers</code>를 입력한 뒤 <strong>Install Plugin</strong>을 선택하시면 돼요.</p>
<h3>Codex App</h3>
<ol>
<li>Codex 앱 내부의 사이드바에서 <strong>Plugins</strong> 메뉴로 가주세요.</li>
<li>코딩 영역(Coding)에 등록되어 있는 <code>Superpowers</code>를 선택해요.</li>
<li>옆에 있는 <code>+</code> 기호를 클릭하고 화면 지침을 이행해 주세요.</li>
</ol>
<h3>Factory Droid</h3>
<p>터미널에서 공식 깃허브 마켓을 등록한 뒤 설치를 진행해요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">droid plugin marketplace add https://github.com/obra/superpowers
droid plugin install superpowers@superpowers
</code></pre>
<h3>Gemini CLI</h3>
<p>구글 제미나이 환경에서는 아래 명령어로 확장(Extension)을 이식해 주세요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">gemini extensions install https://github.com/obra/superpowers
</code></pre>
<h3>OpenCode</h3>
<p>에이전트 입력창에 아래 주소의 인스톨 스크립트를 가져와 실행하라고 문장으로 지시해 주시면 돼요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">Fetch and follow instructions from https://raw.githubusercontent.com/obra/superpowers/refs/heads/main/.opencode/INSTALL.md
</code></pre>
<h3>Cursor</h3>
<p>커서 에이전트 채팅 창에 아래와 같이 짧게 플러그인 등록 명령을 내리거나 마켓에서 직접 찾아볼 수 있어요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">/add-plugin superpowers
</code></pre>
<h3>GitHub Copilot CLI</h3>
<p>깃허브 코필럿 전용 마켓을 지정하고 활성화 명령을 내려줘요.</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">copilot plugin marketplace add obra/superpowers-marketplace
copilot plugin install superpowers@superpowers-marketplace
</code></pre>
<p>기존 코딩 툴에 맞춤형으로 주입해 주기만 하면 사용 준비가 모두 끝나요.</p>

2b:T902,<h2>슈퍼파워가 지휘하는 7단계 개발 여정</h2>
<p>Superpowers가 주입된 에이전트와 매일 코딩을 할 때에는 아래와 같은 7단계 사이클이 알아서 자동으로 흘러가요. 여러분은 각 단계의 체크포인트마다 가볍게 피드백만 주면 돼요.</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>브레인스토밍(Brainstorming)</strong>: 에이전트가 여러분의 모호한 요구 사항을 대화형 질문으로 가다듬고, 검증된 기획 설계 문서를 남겨요.</li>
<li><strong>독립된 작업 공간 격리(Git Worktree)</strong>: 기획이 승인되면 충돌을 막기 위해 깃의 별도 개발 브랜치(가지치기 공간)로 환경을 자동 격리해요.</li>
<li><strong>나노 계획 수립(Writing Plans)</strong>: 단숨에 짤 수 있는 2~5분 단위의 아주 작고 세밀한 할 일 목록으로 설계서를 해체해요.</li>
<li><strong>서브 에이전트 구동(Subagent DD)</strong>: 역할을 쪼갠 보조 인공지능 비서(서브 에이전트)들을 구동해 각 태스크를 수행시켜요.</li>
<li><strong>테스트 주도 개발(TDD)</strong>: "반드시 실패하는 테스트 작성 → 테스트 통과를 위한 최소한의 코드 구현 → 깔끔한 리팩토링(코드 구조 개선)" 순서의 강제적 TDD 순환을 유지해요.</li>
<li><strong>코드 리뷰 요청(Code Review)</strong>: 작성된 코드가 당초 계획했던 의도에 맞는지 자체적인 검수 과정을 통과해야 다음으로 넘어가요.</li>
<li><strong>브랜치 병합 및 정리(Finish Branch)</strong>: 작업이 전부 검증되면 원래의 작업 줄기로 병합(Merge)하고 임시 작업 공간을 말끔히 폐기해요.</li>
</ol>
<h2>작업 시 기억해둘 팁</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>테스트 코드가 최우선이에요</strong>: Superpowers는 테스트 없이 작성되는 무분별한 날림 코드를 차단해요. 에이전트에게 테스트 프레임워크가 정상적으로 잘 잡히는지 첫 기획 대화 단계에서 확인해 주는 것이 좋아요.</li>
<li><strong>언제든 의견 수정하기</strong>: 서브 에이전트들이 도중에 엉뚱한 결정을 내리려고 한다면, 에이전트 메인 대화창에 피드백을 전달해 즉시 계획 수정을 지시할 수 있어요.</li>
</ul>

  GEM --> GeminiMerge["Gemini context merge"]
  HostCtx --> Rule["Skill-before-action mandate"]
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Instruction priority</strong> (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:18-26</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>User explicit instructions (AGENTS.md, direct chat) — <strong>highest</strong></li>
<li>Superpowers skills — override default system on conflict</li>
<li>Default system prompt — lowest</li>
</ol>
<p>Example: user says "skip TDD" → follow user even if <code>test-driven-development</code> says always TDD. This is <strong>policy in markdown</strong>, not code enforcement.</p>
<h3>SessionStart injection (Claude/Cursor/Copilot path)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 162_superpowers/hooks/hooks.json:2-14
"SessionStart": [{
  "matcher": "startup|clear|compact",
  "hooks": [{
    "type": "command",
    "command": "\"${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/hooks/run-hook.cmd\" session-start",
    "async": false
  }]
}]
</code></pre>
<p><code>hooks/session-start:17-35</code> reads <code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md</code> and emits host-specific JSON (<code>additionalContext</code> or Claude hook output format).</p>
<h3>OpenCode path</h3>
<p><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js</code> uses <code>experimental.chat.messages.transform</code> to prepend bootstrap to first user message — different injection slot than Claude SessionStart.</p>

<h2>5. Subagents &#x26; collaboration (005)</h2>
<p>Superpowers defines <strong>workflows in SKILL.md</strong>, not a subagent scheduler.</p>
<h3>5.1 Subagent-driven development (SDD)</h3>
<p><code>skills/subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Principle</strong> (<code>:10-14</code>): Fresh subagent per task + two-stage review (spec then quality)</li>
<li><strong>When to use</strong> (<code>:16-40</code>): Plan exists + independent tasks + same session</li>
<li><strong>Controller discipline</strong>: Never let subagents inherit full session history; paste complete task text inline</li>
<li><strong>Review stages</strong>: Spec compliance reviewer → code quality reviewer</li>
</ul>
<h3>5.2 Parallel dispatch</h3>
<p><code>skills/dispatching-parallel-agents/SKILL.md</code> — independent domain investigations in parallel, then integrate + run full test suite.</p>

<h2>8. Sandbox, config, MCP, memory (007–010, 009)</h2>
<h3>Sandbox (007)</h3>
<p>No <code>--sandbox</code>, seatbelt, allowlist, or command classifier in repo. Skills <strong>reference</strong> host sandbox expectations (e.g., run tests before claiming done) but do not implement isolation.</p>
<p><code>skills/using-git-worktrees/SKILL.md</code> guides isolated workspace creation via host git/worktree commands — policy, not enforcement.</p>
<h3>Config (008)</h3>
<p>Configuration = plugin manifests + host config after install:</p>
<ul>
<li>Codex: <code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code> — skills path, UI metadata</li>
<li>Gemini: <code>gemini-extension.json</code> + <code>GEMINI.md</code> tool map</li>
<li>No layered settings merge engine, no <code>.superpowersrc</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Install paths documented per host in README (Claude marketplace, Codex plugin install, Cursor plugin, etc.).</p>
<h3>MCP (009)</h3>
<p><strong>Negative finding:</strong> No <code>.mcp.json</code>, no stdio MCP server, no OAuth broker, no multi-server orchestration. MCP in other harnesses (if any) comes from host or other plugins — not Superpowers.</p>
<h3>Memory (010)</h3>
<p>Skills are <strong>stateless markdown</strong>. No:</p>
<ul>
<li>Vector index or embeddings</li>
<li>Session fact extraction pipeline</li>
<li><code>MEMORY.md</code> or cross-session replay DB</li>
<li>Compaction-aware memory hooks</li>
</ul>
<p>Persistence is delegated to host session storage + user artifacts (plan docs at <code>docs/superpowers/specs/</code>, git history). <code>verification-before-completion</code> skill mandates evidence artifacts, not automated recall.</p>

36:T5cae,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Superpowers는 방법론을 <strong>Markdown 스킬 + SessionStart 훅</strong>으로 패키징한다. <code>package.json</code>에 <code>bin</code> 필드가 없고, Ratatui/curses/blessed 등 터미널 위젯 스택이 전혀 없다. 사용자가 보는 "TUI"는 100% 호스트 소유이며, Superpowers는 그 세션의 <strong>첫 컨텍스트 슬라이스</strong>와 <strong>스킬 카탈로그</strong>만 제공한다.</p>
<h2>이 문서에서 다루는 것</h2>
<ul>
<li>Architecture</li>
<li>
<ol>
<li>Negative claim: no first-party terminal renderer</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>

<h2>코퍼스 — 001_tui-design/01_sp_tui.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers (<code>sp</code>) — TUI / Terminal UI Design</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0 checkout). <strong>독립 CLI/TUI 없음</strong> — 모든 터미널 렌더링은 호스트 에이전트(Codex, Claude Code, Cursor, OpenCode, Copilot CLI, Gemini CLI)에 위임. Superpowers는 SessionStart 훅과 <code>SKILL.md</code> 부트스트랩으로 호스트 TUI <strong>위에</strong> 방법론 텍스트만 주입한다.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Superpowers는 방법론을 <strong>Markdown 스킬 + SessionStart 훅</strong>으로 패키징한다. <code>package.json</code>에 <code>bin</code> 필드가 없고, Ratatui/curses/blessed 등 터미널 위젯 스택이 전혀 없다. 사용자가 보는 "TUI"는 100% 호스트 소유이며, Superpowers는 그 세션의 <strong>첫 컨텍스트 슬라이스</strong>와 <strong>스킬 카탈로그</strong>만 제공한다.</p>
<p>유일한 "화면"에 가까운 컴포넌트는 <strong>brainstorming visual companion</strong> — 로컬 HTTP/WebSocket으로 HTML mockup을 브라우저에 띄우는 adjunct UI이며, 호스트 TUI를 대체하지 않는다.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TB
  subgraph SP["162_superpowers (no TUI)"]
    Skills["skills/*/SKILL.md"]
    Hook["hooks/session-start"]
    OC[".opencode/plugins/superpowers.js"]
    Brain["brainstorm server.cjs"]
  end

  subgraph HostTUI["Host-owned terminal UI"]
    CodexTUI["Codex TUI / App"]
    CCTUI["Claude Code TUI"]
    CursorTUI["Cursor Agent chat"]
    OCTUI["OpenCode TUI"]
  end

  Skills --> Hook
  Hook -->|JSON context injection| CCTUI
  Hook -->|additional_context| CursorTUI
  Skills --> CodexTUI
  OC -->|first-user-message prepend| OCTUI
  Brain -.->|optional browser tab| Browser["Browser mockups"]
  HostTUI --> User["User reads/writes in host chrome"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Negative claim: no first-party terminal renderer</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Feature</th>
<th>Codex (<code>co</code>)</th>
<th>Superpowers (<code>sp</code>)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Dedicated TUI crate/module</td>
<td><code>codex-rs/tui</code> — panes, status, composer</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>bin</code> CLI entry</td>
<td><code>codex</code> binary</td>
<td><strong>Absent</strong> — <code>package.json</code> only sets OpenCode <code>main</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Terminal widgets</td>
<td>Ratatui layouts, scroll regions</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Session chrome ownership</td>
<td>Codex renders transcript + tool cards</td>
<td>Host renders; SP injects bootstrap text</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Progress/status UI</td>
<td>Host + <code>update_plan</code> / tool output</td>
<td>Skill text only (<code>TodoWrite</code> → host mapping)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Evidence — no binary:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 162_superpowers/package.json:1-6
{
  "name": "superpowers",
  "version": "5.1.0",
  "type": "module",
  "main": ".opencode/plugins/superpowers.js"
}
</code></pre>
<p>Superpowers distribution is a <strong>plugin/skills bundle</strong>, not an executable with its own event loop or frame buffer.</p>

<h2>2. Host routing — who renders the terminal</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Host</th>
<th>Entry manifest</th>
<th>Bootstrap mechanism</th>
<th>TUI owner</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Codex CLI / App</td>
<td><code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code></td>
<td>Native skill discovery via <code>"skills": "./skills/"</code></td>
<td>Codex</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td><code>.claude-plugin/</code> + <code>hooks/hooks.json</code></td>
<td>SessionStart → <code>session-start</code></td>
<td>Claude Code</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cursor</td>
<td><code>.cursor-plugin/plugin.json</code> + <code>hooks/hooks-cursor.json</code></td>
<td>SessionStart (Cursor hook schema)</td>
<td>Cursor</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Copilot CLI</td>
<td>marketplace plugin + hooks</td>
<td><code>additionalContext</code> (SDK standard)</td>
<td>Copilot CLI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode</td>
<td><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js</code></td>
<td><code>experimental.chat.messages.transform</code></td>
<td>OpenCode</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td><code>gemini-extension.json</code> + <code>GEMINI.md</code></td>
<td><code>@import</code> bootstrap + tool map</td>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Codex plugin exposes <strong>marketplace UI metadata</strong> (display name, icons, default prompts) but not terminal layout:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 162_superpowers/.codex-plugin/plugin.json:23-45
"skills": "./skills/",
"interface": {
  "displayName": "Superpowers",
  "shortDescription": "Planning, TDD, debugging, and delivery workflows for coding agents",
  "capabilities": ["Interactive", "Read", "Write"],
  "defaultPrompt": [
    "I've got an idea for something I'd like to build.",
    "Let's add a feature to this project."
  ],
  "composerIcon": "./assets/superpowers-small.svg",
  "logo": "./assets/app-icon.png"
}
</code></pre>
<p>These fields affect <strong>Codex App plugin picker / composer</strong>, not a Superpowers-owned pane.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. SessionStart hook — bootstrap without terminal code</h2>
<p><code>hooks/hooks.json</code> registers SessionStart on <code>startup|clear|compact</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 162_superpowers/hooks/hooks.json:2-14
"SessionStart": [{
  "matcher": "startup|clear|compact",
  "hooks": [{
    "type": "command",
    "command": "\"${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/hooks/run-hook.cmd\" session-start",
    "async": false
  }]
}]
</code></pre>
<p><code>hooks/session-start</code> (<code>:1-57</code>) performs:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Resolve plugin root</strong> from script location (<code>:6-8</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Legacy skills warning</strong> if <code>~/.config/superpowers/skills</code> still exists (<code>:10-15</code>) — tells agent to warn user once.</li>
<li><strong>Read</strong> <code>skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md</code> wholesale (<code>:17-18</code>).</li>
<li><strong>JSON-escape</strong> content via bash parameter substitution (<code>:23-31</code>) — performance fix vs char loop (issue #571).</li>
<li><strong>Wrap</strong> in <code>&#x3C;EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT></code> session fragment (<code>:35</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Platform-branch output</strong> (<code>:46-55</code>):</li>
</ol>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Condition</th>
<th>JSON field</th>
<th>Consumer</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>CURSOR_PLUGIN_ROOT</code> set</td>
<td><code>additional_context</code> (snake_case)</td>
<td>Cursor</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT</code> &#x26;&#x26; !<code>COPILOT_CLI</code></td>
<td><code>hookSpecificOutput.additionalContext</code></td>
<td>Claude Code</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>else (Copilot / unknown)</td>
<td><code>additionalContext</code> (top-level)</td>
<td>Copilot SDK standard</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Claude Code reads <strong>both</strong> snake_case and nested forms without dedup — script emits <strong>only one</strong> to avoid double injection (<code>:41-42</code>).</p>
<p><strong>TUI implication:</strong> injected text appears as <strong>host-managed context</strong> (system/additional context slot), not as a custom Superpowers panel. User still types in host composer; no SP status bar.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. OpenCode — first-user-message injection (TUI-adjacent)</h2>
<p>OpenCode plugin avoids system-message bloat and Qwen multi-system breakage:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">// 162_superpowers/.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:111-133
// Inject bootstrap into the first user message of each session.
// Using a user message instead of a system message avoids:
//   1. Token bloat from system messages repeated every turn (#750)
//   2. Multiple system messages breaking Qwen and other models (#894)
'experimental.chat.messages.transform': async (_input, output) => {
  ...
  firstUser.parts.unshift({ ...ref, type: 'text', text: bootstrap });
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Design choice:</strong> bootstrap renders as if the user pasted methodology preamble — visible in OpenCode transcript as first user bubble prefix, not a separate SP sidebar.</p>
<p>Module-level <code>_bootstrapCache</code> (<code>:49-53</code>, <code>:62-96</code>) avoids re-reading <code>SKILL.md</code> every agent step when OpenCode reloads messages from DB.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Skill activation vs TUI — <code>using-superpowers</code></h2>
<p>Hosts expose native <strong>Skill</strong> tools; SP never draws UI for skill picker:</p>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">// 162_superpowers/skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md:28-36
**In Claude Code:** Use the `Skill` tool...
**In Copilot CLI:** Use the `skill` tool...
**In Gemini CLI:** Skills activate via the `activate_skill` tool.
**In other environments:** Check your platform's documentation...
</code></pre>
<p>Codex mapping (<code>references/codex-tools.md:12</code>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p><code>Skill</code> tool → Skills load natively — just follow the instructions</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Parity:</strong> Codex TUI may show skill invocations as tool cards; Superpowers only supplies <code>SKILL.md</code> bodies — card chrome is Codex-owned.</p>
<p>Subagent guard in bootstrap (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:6-8</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">&#x3C;SUBAGENT-STOP>
If you were dispatched as a subagent to execute a specific task, skip this skill.
&#x3C;/SUBAGENT-STOP>
</code></pre>
<p>Prevents nested bootstrap noise in worker TUI sessions.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Closest non-terminal UI: brainstorm visual companion</h2>
<p>Explicitly <strong>not a TUI</strong> — browser adjunct for mockups while agent continues in host chat.</p>
<h3>6.1 Decision rule (<code>visual-companion.md:7-25</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Use browser</th>
<th>Use terminal (host TUI)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>UI mockups, wireframes</td>
<td>Requirements / scope questions</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Architecture diagrams</td>
<td>Conceptual A/B/C in prose</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Side-by-side visual compare</td>
<td>Tradeoff lists, API design</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Look-and-feel polish</td>
<td>Clarifying questions (word answers)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>"A question <em>about</em> UI is not automatically visual" — wizard <em>type</em> → terminal; wizard <em>layout pick</em> → browser.</p>
<h3>6.2 Session lifecycle (<code>visual-companion.md:33-48</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">scripts/start-server.sh --project-dir /path/to/project
# Returns JSON: port, url, screen_dir, state_dir
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li><strong>Persistence:</strong> <code>--project-dir</code> → <code>.superpowers/brainstorm/&#x3C;session>/</code></li>
<li><strong>Ephemeral:</strong> default <code>/tmp</code> cleaned on stop</li>
<li><strong>User action:</strong> open URL in browser; respond in <strong>terminal</strong> (primary feedback channel)</li>
</ul>
<h3>6.3 Platform-specific process survival (<code>visual-companion.md:50-81</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Platform</th>
<th>Issue</th>
<th>Mitigation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code (Windows)</td>
<td>foreground blocks tool</td>
<td><code>run_in_background: true</code> on Bash</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Codex</td>
<td>reaps background PIDs</td>
<td>script auto-detects <code>CODEX_CI</code>, foreground mode</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td>process lifetime</td>
<td><code>--foreground</code> + <code>is_background: true</code> on shell tool</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Remote/container</td>
<td>localhost unreachable</td>
<td><code>--host 0.0.0.0 --url-host localhost</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>These are <strong>host exec-policy interactions</strong>, not SP TUI features.</p>
<h3>6.4 Server implementation sketch (<code>server.cjs</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Component</th>
<th>Lines (approx)</th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>RFC6455 WebSocket</td>
<td><code>:6-72</code></td>
<td>Live reload on new HTML</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>getNewestScreen()</code></td>
<td><code>:116-125</code></td>
<td>Serve latest <code>.html</code> by mtime</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Frame wrap</td>
<td><code>:107-114</code>, <code>:112-114</code></td>
<td>Fragments → <code>frame-template.html</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Helper inject</td>
<td><code>:101-103</code>, <code>:137-141</code></td>
<td><code>helper.js</code> before <code>&#x3C;/body></code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Inactivity</td>
<td>(later in file)</td>
<td>Auto-exit ~30 min idle</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Agent loop (<code>visual-companion.md:94-126</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Write HTML to <code>screen_dir</code> (Write tool — never cat/heredoc)</li>
<li>Tell user URL + summary; <strong>end turn</strong></li>
<li>Next turn: read <code>state_dir/events</code> JSONL + terminal text</li>
<li>Push <code>waiting.html</code> when returning to text-only steps</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>TUI boundary:</strong> terminal remains host chat; browser is parallel read-only viewport except click selections logged to JSONL.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Cursor manifest drift (TUI-relevant)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">// 162_superpowers/.cursor-plugin/plugin.json:21-24
"skills": "./skills/",
"agents": "./agents/",
"commands": "./commands/",
"hooks": "./hooks/hooks-cursor.json"
</code></pre>
<p><code>agents/</code> and <code>commands/</code> directories are <strong>referenced but absent</strong> in corpus checkout — Cursor may hide missing paths; no SP terminal commands ship from this repo.</p>

<h2>8. Parity matrix vs Codex (<code>co</code>)</h2>
<table>

<td>Bootstrap</td>
<td>system prompt + config.toml</td>

<td>Host keybindings unchanged</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Visual mockups</td>
<td>N/A in core TUI</td>
<td><code>brainstorming</code> HTTP server</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>9. Security / UX notes</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>No cursor overlay:</strong> SP does not draw pointer or highlight in terminal.</li>
<li><strong>Browser companion binds localhost by default</strong> (<code>server.cjs:76-78</code>) — remote setups need explicit <code>--host</code>.</li>
<li><strong>Legacy skills path warning</strong> appears in first agent reply after SessionStart — UX nudge, not TUI modal.</li>
<li><strong>Gitignore reminder:</strong> <code>.superpowers/</code> should be ignored when using project-dir persistence.</li>
</ul>

37:T5324,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>The core prompt-engineering product is <strong><code>using-superpowers</code></strong> — a meta-skill that mandates skill invocation before action — plus workflow skills that embed <strong>subagent prompt templates</strong> and <strong>context curation rules</strong>. Hosts differ in <em>where</em> bootstrap lands (system hook vs first user message vs <code>@import</code> file).</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 002_prompt-context/02_sp_prompt.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — Prompt / Context Surface</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers is a <strong>prompt/context overlay</strong>, not a prompt runtime. It does not construct provider API payloads, compaction transcripts, token budgets, or repository context maps. It injects or registers bootstrap skill text, then relies on the host to load <code>skills/*/SKILL.md</code> bodies on demand.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>The core prompt-engineering product is <strong><code>using-superpowers</code></strong> — a meta-skill that mandates skill invocation before action — plus workflow skills that embed <strong>subagent prompt templates</strong> and <strong>context curation rules</strong>. Hosts differ in <em>where</em> bootstrap lands (system hook vs first user message vs <code>@import</code> file).</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  subgraph Inject["Bootstrap injection"]
    SS["hooks/session-start"]
    OC["OpenCode messages.transform"]
    GEM["GEMINI.md @imports"]
    Codex[".codex-plugin skills path"]
  end

  US["using-superpowers/SKILL.md"] --> SS
  US --> OC
  US --> GEM
  US --> Codex

  SS --> HostCtx["Host context slot"]
  OC --> FirstUser["First user message prefix"]
  GEM --> GeminiCtx["Gemini context file merge"]
  Codex --> NativeSkill["Native skill discovery"]

  HostCtx --> Rule["Mandatory skill-before-action"]
  FirstUser --> Rule
  GeminiCtx --> Rule
  NativeSkill --> Rule

  Rule --> WF["Workflow skills"]
  WF --> Sub["Subagent prompt templates"]
  WF --> Plan["Plan/design doc paths"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. What Superpowers does NOT own (negative claim)</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Capability</th>
<th>Codex / Aider / host</th>
<th>Superpowers</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>System prompt assembly</td>
<td>Host runtime</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Compaction / summarization</td>
<td>Host</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Token budgeting</td>
<td>Host + model</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Repo map / embeddings</td>
<td>Host or Aider RepoMap</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rules / AGENTS.md merge order</td>
<td>Host</td>
<td><strong>Defers</strong> — user files beat skills</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Provider message JSON</td>
<td>Host API layer</td>
<td><strong>None</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Superpowers <strong>shapes behavior through skill text</strong> once the host has loaded it. It is methodology injection, not a context window algorithm.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Instruction priority stack</h2>
<p><code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:18-26</code> defines a three-tier precedence:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>User explicit instructions</strong> — <code>CLAUDE.md</code>, <code>GEMINI.md</code>, <code>AGENTS.md</code>, direct chat requests (<strong>highest</strong>)</li>
<li><strong>Superpowers skills</strong> — override default system behavior on conflict</li>
<li><strong>Default system prompt</strong> — lowest</li>
</ol>
<p>Example: user says "don't use TDD" → follow user even if <code>test-driven-development</code> skill says always TDD.</p>
<p>This is <strong>prompt conflict resolution policy</strong> embedded in bootstrap, not enforced by code.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Bootstrap skill: <code>using-superpowers</code></h2>
<h3>3.1 Mandatory invocation rule (<code>:10-16</code>, <code>:44-46</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">&#x3C;EXTREMELY-IMPORTANT>
If you think there is even a 1% chance a skill might apply...
YOU MUST USE IT.
&#x3C;/EXTREMELY-IMPORTANT>
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Invoke BEFORE any response or action</strong> — including clarifying questions (<code>:85</code>). Skill check precedes exploration.</p>
<h3>3.2 Skill flow graph (<code>:48-75</code>)</h3>
<p>DOT digraph encodes:</p>
<ul>
<li>User message → "Might any skill apply?" → invoke Skill tool (even 1%)</li>
<li>Announce: "Using [skill] to [purpose]"</li>
<li>Checklist skills → <code>TodoWrite</code> per item (host-mapped)</li>
<li>EnterPlanMode path → brainstorming if not already brainstormed</li>
</ul>
<h3>3.3 Red flags table (<code>:78-95</code>)</h3>
<p>Rationalization stop-list: "just a simple question", "need context first", "I'll explore codebase first" — all rejected; skills define <em>how</em> to explore.</p>
<h3>3.4 Skill priority when multiple match (<code>:97-105</code>)</h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>Process skills first</strong> (brainstorming, debugging)</li>
<li><strong>Implementation skills second</strong> (domain-specific)</li>
</ol>
<p>"Let's build X" → brainstorming before frontend skills.</p>
<h3>3.5 Rigid vs flexible skills (<code>:107-113</code>)</h3>
<p>TDD/debugging = rigid; pattern skills = adaptable. Declared inside each skill.</p>
<h3>3.6 Subagent exemption (<code>:6-8</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">&#x3C;SUBAGENT-STOP>
If you were dispatched as a subagent... skip this skill.
&#x3C;/SUBAGENT-STOP>
</code></pre>
<p>Workers should not re-load bootstrap — controller curates their prompt.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. SessionStart hook — Claude/Cursor/Copilot path</h2>
<p><code>hooks/session-start:17-35</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">using_superpowers_content=$(cat "${PLUGIN_ROOT}/skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md" ...)
session_context="&#x3C;EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT>\nYou have superpowers.\n\n**Below is the full content of your 'superpowers:using-superpowers' skill...**\n\n${using_superpowers_escaped}\n..."
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Full SKILL.md body</strong> (including frontmatter) embedded in session context — not a summary.</p>
<p>Platform output (<code>:46-55</code>):</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Platform</th>
<th>JSON shape</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Cursor</td>
<td><code>{ "additional_context": "..." }</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td><code>{ "hookSpecificOutput": { "hookEventName": "SessionStart", "additionalContext": "..." } }</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Copilot / fallback</td>
<td><code>{ "additionalContext": "..." }</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Triggered on <code>startup|clear|compact</code> (<code>hooks/hooks.json:5</code>) — re-injects after compaction clears context.</p>
<p>Legacy warning appended if <code>~/.config/superpowers/skills</code> exists (<code>session-start:12-15</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. OpenCode — first user message prepend</h2>
<p><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:85-93</code> builds bootstrap:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">_bootstrapCache = `&#x3C;EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT>
You have superpowers.
**IMPORTANT: ... Do NOT use the skill tool to load "using-superpowers" again ...**
${content}  // body after frontmatter strip
${toolMapping}
&#x3C;/EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT>`;
</code></pre>
<p>Frontmatter stripped via regex (<code>:16-34</code>) — injection is body-only plus OpenCode tool mapping (<code>:76-83</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Why user message not system</strong> (<code>:111-114</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Avoid system token repeat every turn (#750)</li>
<li>Avoid multiple system messages breaking Qwen (#894)</li>
</ul>
<p>Guard against double injection (<code>:126-129</code>): skip if <code>EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT</code> already in first user parts.</p>
<p>Config hook registers skills path (<code>:103-108</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">config.skills.paths.push(superpowersSkillsDir);
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>6. Gemini — context file imports</h2>
<p><code>GEMINI.md</code> entire content:</p>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">@./skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md
@./skills/using-superpowers/references/gemini-tools.md
</code></pre>
<p>Gemini CLI merges imported files into session context and maps Claude tool names → Gemini tools at load time. Subagent dispatch via <code>@generalist</code> documented in <code>gemini-tools.md:19-39</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Codex — native skill path (no SessionStart hook in tree)</h2>
<p><code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json:23</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">"skills": "./skills/"
</code></pre>
<p>Codex discovers skills from plugin directory; bootstrap skill loaded via native skill mechanism. Tool mapping in <code>references/codex-tools.md</code> — <code>Skill</code> → follow instructions natively; subagents need:</p>
<pre><code class="language-toml"># codex-tools.md:20-23
[features]
multi_agent = true
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>8. Workflow-level prompt engineering</h2>
<h3>8.1 Brainstorming — design-before-code gate</h3>
<p><code>brainstorming/SKILL.md:12-14</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">&#x3C;HARD-GATE>
Do NOT invoke any implementation skill, write any code... until design approved.
&#x3C;/HARD-GATE>
</code></pre>
<p>Checklist (<code>:22-32</code>): context → visual companion offer → questions → approaches → design sections → spec doc → writing-plans.</p>
<p>Design docs path: <code>docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-&#x3C;topic>-design.md</code>.</p>
<h3>8.2 Writing plans — bite-sized tasks</h3>
<p>Plans break work into 2–5 minute tasks with exact paths, complete code snippets, verification steps (README workflow step 3).</p>
<h3>8.3 Subagent context curation (strongest SP prompt design)</h3>
<p><code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:10-14</code>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Subagents should <strong>never inherit</strong> your session's context or history — you construct exactly what they need.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Controller duties:</p>
<ul>
<li>Read plan <strong>once</strong>; extract <strong>full task text</strong> upfront</li>
<li>Provide <strong>scene-setting context</strong> per task</li>
<li>Never make subagent read plan file (<code>:243</code>)</li>
<li>Answer questions before implementation (<code>:252-255</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Prompt templates:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>File</th>
<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>implementer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Task + context + self-review + escalation statuses</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Spec compliance only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Structure/tests/maintainability</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Implementer template (<code>implementer-prompt.md:11-14</code>):</p>
<blockquote>
<p>[FULL TEXT of task from plan - paste it here, don't make subagent read file]</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Status protocol</strong> (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:104-120</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li><code>DONE</code>, <code>DONE_WITH_CONCERNS</code>, <code>NEEDS_CONTEXT</code>, <code>BLOCKED</code> — controller must not ignore escalations.</li>
</ul>
<h3>8.4 Parallel investigation context</h3>
<p><code>dispatching-parallel-agents/SKILL.md:86-110</code> — agent prompts must be:</p>
<ol>
<li>Focused (one domain)</li>
<li>Self-contained (errors pasted inline)</li>
<li>Specific output (summary of root cause + fix)</li>
</ol>
<p>No inherited session history.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Platform tool-name adaptation in prompts</h2>
<p>Skills authored with Claude Code tool names. Reference files rewrite for hosts:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>File</th>
<th>Mappings</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>references/codex-tools.md</code></td>
<td>Task→spawn_agent, TodoWrite→update_plan, Skill→native</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>references/gemini-tools.md</code></td>
<td>Read→read_file, Skill→activate_skill, Task→@generalist</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>references/copilot-tools.md</code></td>
<td>Read→view, Task→task, TodoWrite→sql todos table</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>OpenCode embeds mapping inline in bootstrap (<code>superpowers.js:76-83</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Prompt implication:</strong> same skill body ships everywhere; adaptation layer prevents wrong tool invocation in prompt instructions.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Continuous execution prompt policy</h2>
<p><code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:14</code>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Do not pause to check in with your human partner between tasks... "Should I continue?" prompts waste their time.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>This is <strong>explicit prompt discipline</strong> for controller agents — reduces context churn in host transcript.</p>
<hr>

<h2>코퍼스 — 003_tool-runtime/03_sp_tool.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — Tool Runtime</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers is <strong>not</strong> an independent tool runtime. It does not own shell/file/search/MCP dispatch, approval gates, or structured function-call loops. Its runtime surface is <strong>bootstrap policy + skill catalog + cross-host tool-name adaptation</strong> that teaches the active harness how to interpret Claude Code-oriented skill text.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
  subgraph SP["Superpowers owns"]
    Skills["skills/*/SKILL.md"]
    Bootstrap["using-superpowers"]
    Maps["references/*-tools.md"]
    OCMap["OpenCode inline mapping"]
  end

  subgraph Host["Host owns"]
    Loop["LLM tool loop"]
    Catalog["Tool registry"]
    Dispatch["Tool dispatcher"]
    Approval["Exec approval / sandbox"]
  end

  Skills --> Bootstrap
  Bootstrap --> Agent["Agent reads skill"]
  Agent --> Maps
  Maps --> HostTools["Host-native tool calls"]
  OCMap --> HostTools
  HostTools --> Dispatch
  Dispatch --> Loop
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Classification — ownership table</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Layer</th>
<th>Superpowers owns?</th>
<th>Implementation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>LLM request/response loop</td>
<td><strong>No</strong></td>
<td>Host harness</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool catalog definition</td>
<td><strong>No</strong></td>
<td>Host (Read, Bash, spawn_agent, etc.)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool dispatch / routing</td>
<td><strong>No</strong></td>
<td>Host dispatcher</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool result parsing</td>
<td><strong>No</strong></td>
<td>Host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP server bridge</td>
<td><strong>No</strong></td>
<td>Host or user config</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skill catalog (<code>SKILL.md</code>)</td>
<td><strong>Yes</strong></td>
<td><code>skills/</code> tree</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bootstrap invocation policy</td>
<td><strong>Yes</strong></td>
<td><code>using-superpowers</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tool-name adaptation docs</td>
<td><strong>Yes</strong></td>
<td><code>references/*.md</code>, OpenCode JS</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Behavioral "use TodoWrite" rules</td>
<td><strong>Yes</strong></td>
<td>In skill bodies (host executes)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Negative claim:</strong> Superpowers is not a structured function-call dispatcher, JSON schema registry, or plugin tool loader beyond declaring <code>"skills": "./skills/"</code> in host manifests.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Skills as tool-usage curriculum</h2>
<p><code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:30-36</code> — access patterns:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Host</th>
<th>Skill invocation tool</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td><code>Skill</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Copilot CLI</td>
<td><code>skill</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td><code>activate_skill</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Codex</td>
<td>Native skill load — "just follow the instructions" (<code>codex-tools.md:12</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Critical rule (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:30</code>):</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Never use the Read tool on skill files [in Claude Code].</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Skill tool is the host's dynamic loader; Read bypasses activation metadata.</p>
<p>Flow when checklist present (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:57-74</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Invoke skill</li>
<li>Announce usage</li>
<li>If checklist → create todo per item via host task tracker</li>
<li>Follow skill exactly</li>
</ol>

<pre><code class="language-bash">GIT_DIR=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)

</code></pre>
<p>Signals: linked worktree vs detached HEAD (sandbox).</p>

<p>OpenCode <code>config</code> hook (<code>superpowers.js:103-108</code>) mutates live <code>config.skills.paths</code> — skills discovered lazily without symlinks.</p>
<p><strong>Not tool registration:</strong> paths tell OpenCode where <code>SKILL.md</code> files live; individual tools still come from OpenCode core.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Subagent tools — host-specific dispatch</h2>
<p>Documented in skills, executed by host:</p>
<p><strong>Sequential SDD</strong> (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:50-61</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Dispatch implementer → spec reviewer → code quality reviewer per task</li>
<li><strong>Never</strong> parallel implementers (<code>:242</code>) — file conflict risk</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Parallel debug</strong> (<code>dispatching-parallel-agents/SKILL.md:66-74</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">Task("Fix agent-tool-abort.test.ts failures")
Task("Fix batch-completion-behavior.test.ts failures")
// concurrent
</code></pre>
<p>Codex translation: parallel <code>spawn_agent</code> calls after <code>multi_agent = true</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Brainstorm server — auxiliary process, not agent tools</h2>
<p><code>skills/brainstorming/scripts/server.cjs</code> is a <strong>local HTTP/WebSocket server</strong> for HTML mockups. Invoked via Bash in skill instructions — not registered as host MCP tool by Superpowers.</p>
<p>Agent uses Write tool → files on disk → server serves newest HTML. Tool chain: <strong>host Write + host Bash</strong>, orchestrated by skill prose.</p>
<p>Platform notes (<code>visual-companion.md:67-72</code>): Codex reaps background processes — script detects <code>CODEX_CI</code> for foreground mode.</p>
<hr>

<h2>9. Parity matrix vs Codex (<code>co</code>)</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Concern</th>
<th>Codex (<code>co</code>)</th>
<th>Superpowers (<code>sp</code>)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Tool registry</td>
<td>Rust <code>codex-core</code> tools</td>
<td>Host-only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Shell execution</td>
<td><code>shell</code>, sandbox policy</td>
<td>Skill prose → host Bash</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subagents</td>

<td>Documented in codex-tools.md</td>

<tr>
<td>Plan tracking</td>
<td><code>update_plan</code></td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skill tool</td>
<td>Native load SKILL.md</td>
<td>Provides SKILL.md files</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP</td>
<td>User/server config</td>
<td>Not bundled</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Approval prompts</td>
<td>Codex exec policy</td>
<td>External</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<hr>
<h2>10. Boundary statements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Do not describe Superpowers as executing commands — it <strong>instructs</strong> the host agent to execute.</li>
<li>Tool mappings are <strong>documentation</strong>, not runtime shims (except OpenCode bootstrap text).</li>
<li>Missing host feature (e.g. no <code>multi_agent</code>) → skill workflows <strong>cannot</strong> dispatch subagents; precondition failure is host-side.</li>
<li><code>EnterPlanMode</code> / <code>ExitPlanMode</code> have <strong>no Copilot equivalent</strong> (<code>copilot-tools.md:20</code>) — skills assuming plan mode need controller judgment on Copilot.</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<h2>13. Skill-orchestrated tool sequences (workflow examples)</h2>
<p>Superpowers never registers these as APIs — they are <strong>ordered host tool calls</strong> prescribed in SKILL.md:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Workflow skill</th>
<th>Typical tool chain (Claude names)</th>
<th>Codex mapping</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>brainstorming</code></td>
<td>Read → Skill → Write (spec doc) → optional Bash (start-server.sh)</td>
<td>Same with native file/shell tools</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>writing-plans</code></td>
<td>Read design → Write plan.md → Skill(plan reviewer)</td>
<td>spawn_agent for review optional</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>subagent-driven-development</code></td>
<td>TodoWrite → Task(impl) → Task(spec) → Task(quality) × N</td>
<td>update_plan → spawn_agent × 3 × tasks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>dispatching-parallel-agents</code></td>
<td>Task × N parallel → Read summaries → Bash(test)</td>
<td>spawn_agent × N → wait_agent each</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>test-driven-development</code></td>
<td>Write(test) → Bash(test run) → Write(impl) → Bash(test)</td>
<td>Identical pattern</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>using-git-worktrees</code></td>
<td>Bash(git detect) → native Worktree OR Bash(worktree add)</td>
<td>Sandbox may block worktree Bash</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>finishing-a-development-branch</code></td>
<td>Bash(test) → Bash(git) → user App UI if sandbox blocks</td>
<td>codex-tools.md handoff</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Key insight:</strong> the "runtime" is the agent interpreting skill prose and calling host tools in sequence. No SP scheduler coordinates steps.</p>
<h3>13.1 TodoWrite / update_plan as workflow state machine</h3>
<p><code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:57-74</code> mandates TodoWrite per checklist item when a skill defines a checklist. On Codex this becomes <code>update_plan</code> entries — the host plan UI becomes the <strong>visible state</strong> of skill progress, not an SP database.</p>
<p>Brainstorming checklist has 9 ordered items (<code>brainstorming/SKILL.md:22-32</code>); SDD controller creates todos for <strong>all plan tasks upfront</strong> before first implementer dispatch.</p>
<h3>13.2 Explicit skill requests vs automatic triggering</h3>
<p><code>tests/explicit-skill-requests/</code> validates user saying "use the test-driven-development skill" paths distinct from implicit triggering in <code>tests/skill-triggering/</code>. Both paths still end in host Skill/activate_skill — SP tests document expected harness behavior, not SP dispatch code.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 004_skill-system/04_sp_skill.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — Skill System</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers <strong>is primarily a skill system</strong>: a portable methodology library of <code>skills/*/SKILL.md</code> files plus harness-specific activation glue (SessionStart hooks, Codex plugin manifest, OpenCode JS plugin, Gemini <code>@import</code>s). There is no universal skill VM — loading, permissions, and UI are host-dependent.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
  subgraph Library["skills/ library"]
    US["using-superpowers (bootstrap)"]
    Proc["Process: brainstorming, debugging"]
    Impl["Implementation: TDD, plans, worktrees"]
    Collab["Collaboration: SDD, parallel agents, review"]
    Meta["Meta: writing-skills"]
  end

  subgraph Activation["Host activation"]
    CodexP[".codex-plugin plugin.json"]
    Hook["hooks/session-start"]
    OC["OpenCode superpowers.js"]
    Gem["GEMINI.md imports"]
  end

  US --> Hook
  US --> OC
  US --> Gem
  Library --> CodexP

  CodexP --> HostLoad["Host skill loader"]
  Hook --> HostLoad
  OC --> HostLoad
  Gem --> HostLoad

  HostLoad --> Agent["Agent invokes skills per using-superpowers rules"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Core model — SKILL.md schema</h2>
<h3>1.1 File layout</h3>
<ul>
<li>Each first-party skill: <code>skills/&#x3C;kebab-name>/SKILL.md</code></li>
<li>Colocated assets: prompt templates (<code>*.md</code>), scripts (<code>scripts/</code>), references (<code>references/</code>)</li>
<li>Observed YAML frontmatter:</li>
</ul>
<pre><code class="language-yaml">---
name: using-superpowers
description: Use when starting any conversation - establishes how to find and use skills...
---
</code></pre>
<p>Required fields in practice: <code>name</code>, <code>description</code> (used for discovery/triggering).</p>
<h3>1.2 Bootstrap skill</h3>
<p><code>using-superpowers</code> is the <strong>meta-skill</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Mandates skill invocation before any action (<code>SKILL.md:10-16</code>)</li>
<li>Defines instruction priority vs user AGENTS.md (<code>:18-26</code>)</li>
<li>Platform Skill tool access (<code>:28-36</code>)</li>
<li>Skill flow DOT graph (<code>:48-75</code>)</li>
<li>Red-flag rationalization table (<code>:78-95</code>)</li>
<li>Subagent skip gate (<code>:6-8</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Embedded wholesale by <code>hooks/session-start:17-35</code> on SessionStart.</p>
<h3>1.3 Skill types (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:107-113</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Examples</th>
<th>Agent behavior</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Rigid</strong></td>
<td>TDD, systematic-debugging</td>
<td>Follow exactly</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Flexible</strong></td>
<td>Pattern skills</td>
<td>Adapt principles</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Declared per skill, not in central schema registry.</p>

<hr>
<h2>3. Representative skill internals</h2>
<h3>3.1 brainstorming (<code>skills/brainstorming/SKILL.md</code>)</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>&#x3C;HARD-GATE></code> blocks all implementation until design approved (<code>:12-14</code>)</li>
<li>9-item checklist with TodoWrite per item (<code>:22-32</code>)</li>
<li>Spec output: <code>docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-&#x3C;topic>-design.md</code></li>
<li>Visual companion optional branch (<code>visual-companion.md</code>)</li>
<li>Server scripts: <code>scripts/server.cjs</code>, <code>start-server.sh</code>, <code>stop-server.sh</code></li>
</ul>
<h3>3.2 test-driven-development</h3>
<p>Iron Law (<code>SKILL.md:33-35</code>):</p>
<pre><code>NO PRODUCTION CODE WITHOUT A FAILING TEST FIRST
</code></pre>
<p>Write code before test → delete and restart (<code>:37-45</code>). Includes testing anti-patterns reference in tree.</p>
<h3>3.3 systematic-debugging</h3>
<p>Iron Law (<code>SKILL.md:18-20</code>):</p>
<pre><code>NO FIXES WITHOUT ROOT CAUSE INVESTIGATION FIRST
</code></pre>
<p>Four phases: investigation → hypothesis → fix → verification. Sub-references: root-cause-tracing, defense-in-depth, condition-based-waiting.</p>
<h3>3.4 subagent-driven-development</h3>
<p>Support files:</p>

<th>Role</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<tr>
<td><code>implementer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Full task text + escalation statuses</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Spec compliance review</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code></td>
<td>Quality review</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Integration deps (<code>SKILL.md:268-279</code>): worktrees, writing-plans, requesting-code-review, finishing branch, TDD for implementers.</p>
<h3>3.5 writing-plans</h3>
<p>Includes <code>plan-document-reviewer-prompt.md</code> for plan quality review before execution.</p>
<h3>3.6 writing-skills (meta)</h3>
<p>References:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>anthropic-best-practices.md</code></li>
<li><code>persuasion-principles.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Contribution guide (<code>README.md:207-217</code>): new skills via <code>writing-skills</code> skill; must work cross-harness.</p>

<h3>4.1 Codex plugin metadata (<code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "name": "superpowers",

  "keywords": ["brainstorming", "subagent-driven-development", "tdd", "debugging"],

<h3>4.3 OpenCode plugin (most concrete in-repo adapter)</h3>

<li><code>config</code> hook — append skills dir to <code>config.skills.paths</code> (<code>:103-108</code>)</li>

<h3>4.4 Cursor manifest note</h3>
<p><code>.cursor-plugin/plugin.json</code> references <code>./agents/</code> and <code>./commands/</code> — <strong>directories absent</strong> in checkout; skills path valid.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Skill discovery and triggering policy</h2>
<h3>5.1 Mandatory check (<code>using-superpowers</code>)</h3>
<p>Before <strong>any</strong> response including clarifications — invoke Skill tool if ≥1% applicability.</p>
<p>Priority when multiple skills (<code>:97-105</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Process (brainstorm, debug)</li>
<li>Implementation</li>
</ol>
<h3>5.2 Brainstorming auto-path</h3>
<p>If entering plan mode without prior brainstorm → invoke brainstorming first (flow graph <code>:62-65</code>).</p>
<h3>5.3 Tests</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Directory</th>
<th>Purpose</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>

<h2>6. Legacy skills path migration</h2>
<p><code>hooks/session-start:12-15</code> warns if <code>~/.config/superpowers/skills</code> exists — superseded by host-native skill dirs (e.g. <code>~/.claude/skills</code>). One-time agent message to user on first reply.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 005_subagents-collab/05_sp_subagent.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — Subagents / Collaboration</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers defines <strong>subagent collaboration workflows in SKILL.md</strong>, not a native subagent runtime. Spawn, lifecycle, context isolation, async completion, parallelism limits, and model routing are <strong>delegated to the active host harness</strong>. SP's contribution is precise prompt templates, controller discipline, and host tool-name mapping.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TB
  Controller["Controller agent (main session)"]

  subgraph SDD["subagent-driven-development (sequential)"]
    Imp["Implementer subagent"]
    SpecR["Spec reviewer"]
    QualR["Code quality reviewer"]
  end

  subgraph Parallel["dispatching-parallel-agents"]
    A1["Agent domain A"]
    A2["Agent domain B"]
    A3["Agent domain C"]
  end

  Plan["writing-plans output"] --> Controller
  Controller --> Imp
  Imp --> SpecR
  SpecR --> QualR
  QualR --> Controller

  Controller --> A1
  Controller --> A2
  Controller --> A3
  A1 --> Integrate["Review + merge + test suite"]
  A2 --> Integrate
  A3 --> Integrate
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Negative claim — no SP subagent engine</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Capability</th>
<th>Owner</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>spawn_agent</code> / <code>Task</code> / <code>@generalist</code> dispatch</td>
<td>Host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Context isolation between workers</td>
<td>Host (best-effort)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subagent depth limits</td>
<td>Host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Parallel execution scheduler</td>
<td>Host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worker transcript storage</td>
<td>Host</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Review prompt <strong>content</strong></td>
<td>Superpowers SKILL.md + templates</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Controller workflow rules</td>
<td>Superpowers</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Superpowers <strong>cannot guarantee</strong> technical isolation — it requires the controller to <strong>never</strong> let subagents inherit session history and to paste <strong>full task text</strong> inline.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Core pattern: subagent-driven development (SDD)</h2>
<p><code>skills/subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md</code></p>
<h3>2.1 Principle (<code>:10-14</code>)</h3>
<blockquote>
<p>Fresh subagent per task + two-stage review (spec then quality) = high quality, fast iteration</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Why subagents</strong> (<code>:10-11</code>): delegate with <strong>constructed</strong> instructions; preserve controller context for coordination.</p>
<p><strong>Continuous execution</strong> (<code>:14</code>): no "should I continue?" between tasks — only stop if BLOCKED, ambiguous, or done.</p>
<h3>2.2 When to use vs alternatives (<code>:16-40</code>)</h3>
<p>Decision graph:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Condition</th>
<th>Choose</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Plan + independent tasks + same session</td>
<td><strong>subagent-driven-development</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Plan + parallel separate session</td>
<td><strong>executing-plans</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No plan</td>
<td>brainstorm / manual first</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>2.3 Per-task pipeline (<code>:44-86</code>)</h3>
<ol>
<li>Controller reads plan once; extracts <strong>all tasks with full text</strong>; TodoWrite all</li>
<li>Dispatch <strong>implementer</strong> (<code>implementer-prompt.md</code>)</li>
<li>Implementer may ask questions <strong>before</strong> coding — controller answers (<code>:252-255</code>)</li>
<li>Implementer implements, tests, commits, <strong>self-reviews</strong></li>
<li>Dispatch <strong>spec reviewer</strong> — spec compliance ONLY</li>
<li>If fail → implementer fixes → re-review spec</li>
<li><strong>Only after spec ✅</strong> → dispatch <strong>code quality reviewer</strong></li>
<li>If fail → fix → re-review quality</li>
<li>Mark todo complete; next task</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Order violation red flag</strong> (<code>:249</code>): never start quality review before spec compliance.</p>
<p><strong>Parallelism red flag</strong> (<code>:242</code>): never dispatch multiple <strong>implementers</strong> concurrently — file conflicts.</p>
<h3>2.4 Implementer status protocol (<code>:104-120</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Status</th>
<th>Controller action</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>DONE</code></td>
<td>Proceed to spec review</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>DONE_WITH_CONCERNS</code></td>
<td>Read concerns; address if correctness/scope</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>NEEDS_CONTEXT</code></td>
<td>Provide missing context; re-dispatch</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>BLOCKED</code></td>
<td>Context fix, bigger model, split task, or escalate human</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Never retry same model without changes after BLOCKED.</p>
<h3>2.5 Model selection (<code>:89-102</code>)</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Task signal</th>
<th>Model tier</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>1-2 files, complete spec</td>
<td>Fast/cheap</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Multi-file integration</td>
<td>Standard</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Architecture/review</td>
<td>Most capable</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Cost tradeoff (<code>:230-234</code>): more invocations (impl + 2 reviewers × N tasks) vs fewer late bugs.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Prompt templates — context curation</h2>
<h3>3.1 Implementer (<code>implementer-prompt.md</code>)</h3>
<p>Structure:</p>
<pre><code>Task tool (general-purpose):
  description: "Implement Task N: [task name]"
  prompt: |
    ## Task Description
    [FULL TEXT - don't make subagent read file]

    ## Context
    [Scene-setting: dependencies, architecture]

    ## Before You Begin
    Ask questions now...

    ## Your Job
    1. Implement exactly
    2. Write tests (TDD if specified)
    3. Verify, commit, self-review
    4. Report status: DONE | DONE_WITH_CONCERNS | NEEDS_CONTEXT | BLOCKED
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Scene-setting</strong> mandatory (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:244</code>).</p>
<p><strong>Escalation</strong> (<code>implementer-prompt.md:57-72</code>): BLOCKED when architectural decisions, unbounded reading, plan mismatch.</p>
<p><strong>File scope</strong> (<code>:44-55</code>): follow plan structure; report DONE_WITH_CONCERNS if files grow beyond intent.</p>
<h3>3.2 Spec reviewer (<code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code>)</h3>
<p>Verifies requirements met, nothing extra — before quality review.</p>
<h3>3.3 Code quality reviewer (<code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code>)</h3>
<p>Structure, tests, maintainability — only after spec ✅.</p>
<h3>3.4 Final reviewer</h3>
<p>After all tasks — entire implementation review before <code>finishing-a-development-branch</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Parallel pattern: dispatching-parallel-agents</h2>
<p><code>skills/dispatching-parallel-agents/SKILL.md</code></p>
<h3>4.1 Use when (<code>:36-45</code>)</h3>
<ul>
<li>3+ test files / subsystems failing <strong>independently</strong></li>
<li>No shared state between investigations</li>
<li>Domains understood without cross-context</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Don't use</strong> when failures related, exploratory unknown root cause, or agents would edit same files.</p>
<h3>4.2 Pattern (<code>:47-82</code>)</h3>
<ol>
<li>Group failures by domain</li>
<li>Craft focused prompts (scope, goal, constraints, output format)</li>
<li>Dispatch parallel Tasks</li>
<li>Integrate: read summaries, conflict check, full test suite</li>
</ol>
<p>Example prompt shape (<code>:91-110</code>): paste failing test names, errors, constraints ("Do NOT just increase timeouts").</p>
<h3>4.3 Real session example (<code>:133-158</code>)</h3>
<p>6 failures → 3 agents → independent fixes → full green, zero conflicts.</p>
<p><strong>Contrast with SDD:</strong> parallel <strong>investigation</strong>, not parallel <strong>implementation</strong>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Host tool mapping for subagents</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Host</th>
<th>Dispatch</th>
<th>Wait/result</th>
<th>Parallel</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td><code>Task</code></td>
<td>returns to session</td>
<td>Multiple <code>Task</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Codex</td>
<td><code>spawn_agent</code></td>
<td><code>wait_agent</code>, <code>close_agent</code></td>
<td>Multiple spawn (needs <code>multi_agent</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini</td>
<td><code>@generalist</code> + filled template</td>
<td>agent completes in thread</td>
<td>Same-prompt multi @</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode</td>
<td><code>@mention</code> subagent</td>
<td>host-specific</td>
<td>host-specific</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Copilot</td>
<td><code>task</code> + <code>agent_type</code></td>
<td><code>read_agent</code>, <code>list_agents</code></td>
<td>Multiple <code>task</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>From <code>references/codex-tools.md:5-14</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-toml">[features]
multi_agent = true
</code></pre>
<p>From <code>references/gemini-tools.md:25-31</code>: named skill agents map to <code>@generalist</code> or <code>@code-reviewer</code> with filled template.</p>
<p>From <code>references/copilot-tools.md:15-18</code>: <code>task</code> with <code>general-purpose</code> or <code>explore</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Integration with other skills</h2>
<p>SDD required workflow skills (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:268-279</code>):</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Skill</th>

</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>using-git-worktrees</code></td>
<td>Isolated workspace before execution</td>

<td><code>requesting-code-review</code></td>
<td>Reviewer subagent templates</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>finishing-a-development-branch</code></td>
<td>Post-SDD merge/PR</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>test-driven-development</code></td>
<td>Implementer discipline</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Alternative: <code>executing-plans</code> for <strong>parallel session</strong> with human checkpoints between batches.</p>
<p>Code review axis:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>requesting-code-review</code> — pre-review checklist, <code>code-reviewer.md</code></li>
<li><code>receiving-code-review</code> — systematic response to human review</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>7. SDD example narrative (<code>SKILL.md:128-201</code>)</h2>
<p>Walkthrough: 5 tasks, implementer asks hook install level, spec reviewer catches extra <code>--json</code> flag, quality reviewer catches magic number — demonstrates <strong>review loops</strong> and re-dispatch same implementer for fixes.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. Red flags summary (<code>:236-265</code>)</h2>
<p><strong>Never:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Skip spec OR quality review</li>
<li>Parallel implementers</li>
<li>Subagent reads plan file</li>
<li>Skip scene-setting context</li>
<li>Accept "close enough" on spec issues</li>
<li>Implementer self-review replaces human-style reviewer subagents</li>
<li>Move to next task with open review issues</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>If reviewer finds issues:</strong> implementer fixes → reviewer re-reviews until ✅.</p>
<p><strong>If stuck:</strong> dispatch fix subagent — controller should not patch manually (context pollution).</p>
<hr>

<h2>13. Controller anti-patterns (collaboration failures)</h2>
<p>Documented red flags (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:236-265</code>) with operational meaning:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Anti-pattern</th>
<th>Why it breaks collaboration</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Subagent reads plan file</td>
<td>Worker wastes context tokens; may skim miss tasks</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Controller patches after failed impl</td>
<td>Pollutes controller context; violates fix-subagent dispatch</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Parallel implementers</td>
<td>Merge conflicts; reviewers cannot attribute changes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skip spec review</td>
<td>Over/under-build reaches quality review undetected</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Quality review before spec</td>
<td>Wrong gate order — aesthetic polish on wrong behavior</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ignore BLOCKED status</td>
<td>Repeated failure without model/context/task change</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Should I continue?" mid-plan</td>
<td>Violates continuous execution contract (<code>:14</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>dispatching-parallel-agents</strong> adds integration step (<code>SKILL.md:168-173</code>): after parallel return, controller must run <strong>full test suite</strong> — partial green is insufficient.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 006_app-server-client-surfaces/06_sp_surface.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — App Server / Client Surfaces</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers is a <strong>multi-harness skills/plugin distribution</strong>, not a general app-server agent runtime. The host agent owns model calls, session storage, primary UI, tool execution, subagent dispatch, and permissions. SP exposes <strong>plugin manifests</strong>, <strong>SessionStart hooks</strong>, <strong>OpenCode JS plugin</strong>, and one optional <strong>local HTTP/WebSocket visual companion</strong> for brainstorming.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TB
  subgraph Hosts["Host surfaces (primary)"]
    Codex["Codex CLI / App + plugin market"]
    CC["Claude Code plugin"]
    Cur["Cursor plugin"]
    Cop["Copilot CLI marketplace"]
    Gem["Gemini extension"]
    OC["OpenCode plugin JS"]
  end

  subgraph SP["Superpowers artifacts"]
    Skills["skills/"]
    Hooks["hooks/"]
    Manifests[".*-plugin/ plugin.json"]
    Brain["brainstorm server.cjs"]
  end

  Skills --> Manifests
  Hooks --> CC
  Hooks --> Cur
  Manifests --> Codex
  Manifests --> Cur
  OC --> OC
  Gem --> Gem
  Brain -.-> Browser["Browser tab (optional)"]

  Hosts --> User["User session"]
  Brain -.-> User
</code></pre>
<hr>

<h2>3. Codex plugin surface (<code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code>)</h2>
<p>Full interface block for <strong>Codex App marketplace UI</strong>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">"interface": {
  "displayName": "Superpowers",
  "shortDescription": "Planning, TDD, debugging, and delivery workflows for coding agents",
  "longDescription": "Use Superpowers to guide agent work through brainstorming...",
  "capabilities": ["Interactive", "Read", "Write"],
  "defaultPrompt": [
    "I've got an idea for something I'd like to build.",
    "Let's add a feature to this project."
  ],
  "brandColor": "#F59E0B",
  "composerIcon": "./assets/superpowers-small.svg",
  "logo": "./assets/app-icon.png"
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Client impact:</strong> plugin picker, composer icon, default prompts — not a separate Superpowers window.</p>
<p>Codex install (<code>README.md:63-87</code>): <code>/plugins</code> → search <code>superpowers</code> → Install; App sidebar Plugins → Coding section.</p>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> upstream removed Codex-specific hooks branch (<code>remove-codex-hooks</code>) — activation is skills-directory native, not SessionStart shell hook.</p>

<h2>4. Claude Code surface</h2>
<h3>4.1 Plugin metadata (<code>.claude-plugin/plugin.json</code>)</h3>
<p>Name, description, version 5.1.0, keywords — no skills path in this minimal JSON (skills ship in bundle layout per Claude conventions).</p>
<h3>4.2 Hooks (<code>hooks/hooks.json</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">"SessionStart": [{
  "matcher": "startup|clear|compact",
  "hooks": [{
    "type": "command",
    "command": "\"${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/hooks/run-hook.cmd\" session-start"
  }]
}]
</code></pre>
<p><code>hooks/session-start</code> emits platform-specific JSON (<code>additionalContext</code> / <code>hookSpecificOutput</code>).</p>

<p>Install path: agent fetches <code>.opencode/INSTALL.md</code> from GitHub raw URL (<code>README.md:122-126</code>).</p>
<p>Detailed docs: <code>docs/README.opencode.md</code>.</p>
<h3>7.3 Design constraints documented in source</h3>
<ul>
<li>Bootstrap cached module-level (<code>#1202</code>)</li>
<li>Skip double injection if <code>EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT</code> present (<code>:126-129</code>)</li>
<li>User message not system — Qwen + token bloat issues</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>8. Copilot CLI surface</h2>
<p>Marketplace:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">copilot plugin marketplace add obra/superpowers-marketplace
copilot plugin install superpowers@superpowers-marketplace
</code></pre>
<p>SessionStart uses top-level <code>additionalContext</code> when <code>COPILOT_CLI=1</code> (<code>session-start:52-54</code>).</p>
<p>Tool mapping: <code>references/copilot-tools.md</code> — includes async bash sessions, <code>sql</code> todos, GitHub MCP tools.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Visual companion — local HTTP/WebSocket server</h2>
<p><strong>Only SP-owned network server</strong> in core repo. Not an agent execution service.</p>
<h3>9.1 Purpose (<code>visual-companion.md:1-25</code>)</h3>
<p>Browser mockups for brainstorming — agent stays in host chat; user opens localhost URL.</p>
<h3>9.2 Start session (<code>visual-companion.md:35-42</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">scripts/start-server.sh --project-dir /path/to/project
# JSON: port, url, screen_dir, state_dir
</code></pre>
<p>Persistence: <code>&#x3C;project>/.superpowers/brainstorm/&#x3C;session-id>/</code>.</p>

<h3>9.4 Interaction loop</h3>
<ol>
<li>Agent Write → <code>screen_dir/*.html</code></li>
<li>User views browser; clicks logged to <code>state_dir/events</code> JSONL</li>
<li>User <strong>replies in terminal</strong> — primary feedback</li>
<li>Agent reads events + terminal text next turn</li>
</ol>
