<h2>코퍼스 — 007_sandbox-exec-policy/07_sp_sandbox.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers — Sandbox / Exec Policy</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code> (v5.1.0). Superpowers is a <strong>skills/bootstrap package</strong>, not an execution harness. It does <strong>not</strong> enforce OS process isolation, command approval UI, filesystem ACLs, network filtering, PTY sandboxing, or shell policy evaluation. Actual execution, sandbox seatbelts, and approval prompts are <strong>host-owned</strong>. SP improves <strong>process safety through behavioral skills</strong> (TDD, debugging, worktrees, verification) — not kernel-level confinement.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
  subgraph SP["Superpowers (behavioral)"]
    TDD["test-driven-development"]
    Debug["systematic-debugging"]
    WT["using-git-worktrees"]
    Verify["verification-before-completion"]
    Finish["finishing-a-development-branch"]
  end

  subgraph Host["Host (enforcement)"]
    Sandbox["OS sandbox / seatbelt"]
    Approval["Exec approval prompts"]
    Policy["allow/deny rules"]
    Shell["Shell/PTY execution"]
  end

  SP -->|skill text instructs| Agent["Agent"]
  Agent --> Shell
  Shell --> Sandbox
  Sandbox --> Policy
  Policy --> Approval
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Ownership boundary table</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Area</th>
<th>Owner</th>
<th>SP mechanism</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Skill files &#x26; workflow prose</td>
<td>Superpowers</td>
<td><code>skills/*/SKILL.md</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bootstrap context injection</td>
<td>Superpowers</td>
<td>hooks / plugin</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Shell/file/tool execution</td>
<td><strong>Host</strong></td>
<td>Native tools</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sandbox (landlock/seatbelt/etc.)</td>
<td><strong>Host</strong></td>
<td>Codex, Claude, etc.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network egress policy</td>
<td><strong>Host</strong></td>
<td>—</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Command allowlists</td>
<td><strong>Host</strong></td>
<td>—</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subagent isolation</td>
<td><strong>Host</strong></td>
<td>Best-effort</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Git worktree isolation</td>
<td><strong>Git + skill guidance</strong></td>
<td>Not OS sandbox</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Don't skip TDD" discipline</td>
<td>Superpowers skill</td>
<td>Prompt-only</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Absences verified:</strong> no seatbelt, bwrap, seccomp, landlock, chroot, firewall, or policy evaluator code in <code>162_superpowers/</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>2. Codex plugin capabilities — not sandbox policy</h2>
<p><code>.codex-plugin/plugin.json:30-34</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">"capabilities": ["Interactive", "Read", "Write"]
</code></pre>
<p>Marketplace <strong>capability labels</strong> for plugin listing — not exec policy rules. No sandbox configuration in plugin JSON.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Host exec policy delegation</h2>
<h3>3.1 Codex App sandbox constraints (<code>codex-tools.md:49-59</code>)</h3>
<p>Documented as <strong>external host behavior</strong> in skill reference:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>When the sandbox blocks branch/push operations (detached HEAD in externally managed worktree)...</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Agent workflow:</p>
<ul>
<li>Commit work locally</li>
<li>Inform user to use App UI: <strong>"Create branch"</strong> or <strong>"Hand off to local"</strong></li>
<li>Still run tests, stage, suggest branch name / PR description</li>
</ul>
<p>SP <strong>documents adaptation</strong>; Codex App enforces sandbox.</p>
<h3>3.2 Environment detection before mutating git</h3>
<p><code>codex-tools.md:34-47</code> — read-only git introspection:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">GIT_DIR=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)
GIT_COMMON=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-common-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)
BRANCH=$(git branch --show-current)
</code></pre>
<p>Signals:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>GIT_DIR != GIT_COMMON</code> → linked worktree (skip create)</li>
<li><code>BRANCH</code> empty → detached HEAD (branch/push blocked in sandbox)</li>
</ul>
<p>Used by <code>using-git-worktrees</code> Step 0 and <code>finishing-a-development-branch</code> Step 1.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. using-git-worktrees — sandbox interaction</h2>
<p><code>skills/using-git-worktrees/SKILL.md</code></p>
<h3>4.1 Native-first (<code>:47-57</code>)</h3>
<p>Prefer host native worktree tools (<code>EnterWorktree</code>, <code>/worktree</code>, <code>--worktree</code>) over manual <code>git worktree add</code> — avoids <strong>phantom state</strong> harness cannot manage.</p>
<h3>4.2 Sandbox fallback (<code>:112</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">If `git worktree add` fails with a permission error (sandbox denial), tell the user
the sandbox blocked worktree creation and you're working in the current directory instead.
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Explicit fail-soft:</strong> report sandbox block; continue in place — not bypass.</p>
<h3>4.3 Safety verification (<code>:85-97</code>)</h3>
<p>Project-local <code>.worktrees/</code> must be gitignored before creation — prevents accidental commit of worktree contents. Behavioral guard, not sandbox.</p>
<h3>4.4 Submodule guard (<code>:26-31</code>)</h3>
<p><code>GIT_DIR != GIT_COMMON</code> also true in submodules — must check <code>git rev-parse --show-superproject-working-tree</code> before skipping worktree creation.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Behavioral safety skills (prompt-enforced)</h2>
<h3>5.1 test-driven-development</h3>
<p>Iron Law (<code>SKILL.md:33-35</code>):</p>
<pre><code>NO PRODUCTION CODE WITHOUT A FAILING TEST FIRST
</code></pre>
<p>Delete any code written before tests (<code>:37-45</code>). Reduces reckless edits; <strong>does not</strong> restrict shell commands.</p>
<h3>5.2 systematic-debugging</h3>
<p>Iron Law (<code>SKILL.md:18-20</code>):</p>
<pre><code>NO FIXES WITHOUT ROOT CAUSE INVESTIGATION FIRST
</code></pre>
<p>Four phases before fixes. Under time pressure — still mandatory (<code>:34-44</code>).</p>
<p>Techniques in tree: root-cause-tracing, defense-in-depth, condition-based-waiting — investigation discipline, not syscall filtering.</p>
<h3>5.3 verification-before-completion</h3>
<p>Ensures fixes verified with evidence before claiming done — reduces false "fixed" reports.</p>
<h3>5.4 requesting-code-review / subagent-driven-development</h3>
<p>Two-stage review (spec then quality) — prevents shipping spec violations; enforced by <strong>workflow</strong>, not permissions.</p>
<p>Red flags (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:236-250</code>): skip reviews, parallel implementers, proceed on main without consent.</p>
<h3>5.5 finishing-a-development-branch</h3>
<p>Structured merge/PR/discard — coordinates git operations within host sandbox limits.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Brainstorm server — local network exposure</h2>
<p><code>server.cjs:76-78</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">const PORT = process.env.BRAINSTORM_PORT || (49152 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 16383));
const HOST = process.env.BRAINSTORM_HOST || '127.0.0.1';
</code></pre>
<p>Default <strong>localhost bind</strong> — not a sandbox, but reduces exposure. Remote setups: <code>--host 0.0.0.0 --url-host localhost</code> (<code>visual-companion.md:83-92</code>).</p>
<p>Agent instructed to use <strong>Write tool</strong> for HTML — not shell heredoc (<code>visual-companion.md:100</code>) — reduces shell injection noise, not security boundary.</p>
<p>Inactivity auto-shutdown ~30 min — resource limit, not policy engine.</p>
<hr>
<h2>7. Hooks and plugins — no exec side effects</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Component</th>
<th>Exec impact</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>hooks/session-start</code></td>
<td>Reads SKILL.md, prints JSON — no subprocess spawn of user code</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js</code></td>
<td>Config + message transform only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>hooks/hooks.json</code></td>
<td>Invokes session-start via <code>run-hook.cmd</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>No approval evaluator in hook chain.</p>
<hr>
<h2>8. OpenCode / Copilot / Gemini — policy external</h2>
<ul>
<li>OpenCode: skill path registration only — exec policy is OpenCode core</li>
<li>Copilot: <code>bash</code> with optional <code>async: true</code> — async session tools documented in <code>copilot-tools.md:22-32</code>; approval is Copilot's</li>
<li>Gemini: <code>run_shell_command</code> — Gemini CLI policy</li>
</ul>
<p>Superpowers maps tool names; <strong>never intercepts</strong> command strings.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Subagent exec isolation</h2>
<p>SP requires fresh subagent per task with curated prompt (<code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:10-11</code>) — limits <strong>context leakage</strong>, not syscall access.</p>
<p>Workers inherit <strong>host sandbox</strong> of subagent runtime. SP cannot restrict subagent shell beyond host rules.</p>
<p><strong>Forbidden:</strong> parallel implementers (<code>:242</code>) — reduces file conflict race, not security ACL.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. What README claims vs exec</h2>
<p><code>README.md:9-19</code> describes methodology (brainstorm → plan → SDD → review) — no mention of OS sandboxing, approvals, or network policy.</p>
<p>Philosophy (<code>:199-203</code>): TDD, systematic process, simplicity, evidence — all <strong>behavioral</strong>.</p>
<hr>

<hr>
<h2>12. Failure modes and reporting obligations</h2>
<p>Skills mandate <strong>reporting</strong> sandbox/precondition failures verbatim (AGENTS-style), not silent fallback:</p>
<ul>
<li>Worktree permission denied → tell user (<code>using-git-worktrees</code>)</li>
<li>Detached HEAD blocks push → Codex App UI handoff (<code>codex-tools.md</code>)</li>
<li>BLOCKED subagent → escalate, don't retry blindly (<code>subagent-driven-development</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Aligns with "fail fast" orchestration — behavioral analog to exec policy deny.</p>

<h2>15. executing-plans vs SDD — human gate as exec policy analog</h2>
<p><code>executing-plans</code> skill activates when plan execution happens in a <strong>parallel session</strong> with <strong>human checkpoints</strong> between batches — an explicit <strong>human-in-the-loop approval</strong> between tool bursts. SDD (<code>subagent-driven-development</code>) removes inter-task human gates (<code>:14</code>) relying instead on automated reviewer subagents.</p>
<p>Neither mode changes OS sandbox; the difference is <strong>who approves continuation</strong> (human vs reviewer Task).</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Mode</th>
<th>Approval between tasks</th>
<th>Isolation</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>executing-plans</td>
<td>Human checkpoint</td>
<td>Separate session</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>subagent-driven-development</td>
<td>Spec + quality subagents</td>
<td>Same session, fresh subagent context</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Manual (no skill)</td>
<td>Ad hoc</td>
<td>User responsibility</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>15.1 Git operations under sandbox — finishing branch</h3>
<p><code>finishing-a-development-branch</code> coordinates test verification before merge/PR/discard. When host sandbox blocks <code>git push</code> or branch creation, skill defers to Codex App UI paths documented in <code>codex-tools.md:49-59</code> — agent still allowed: stage, commit, run tests, emit suggested commands for user copy-paste.</p>
<h3>15.2 No SP override of host "never" rules</h3>
<p>Instruction priority (<code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:18-26</code>) ensures user AGENTS.md beats skills. If user configures host exec policy or rules file saying "never run destructive commands," Superpowers skills cannot override — behavioral TDD does not trump explicit user deny rules.</p>

<h2>2. OpenCode Runtime Config (in-repo mutation)</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js</code> (135 lines).</p>
<h3>2.1 Skills path injection (<code>:103-108</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">config: async (config) => {
  config.skills = config.skills || {};
  config.skills.paths = config.skills.paths || [];
  if (!config.skills.paths.includes(superpowersSkillsDir)) {
    config.skills.paths.push(superpowersSkillsDir);
  }
},
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li><code>superpowersSkillsDir</code> = <code>path.resolve(__dirname, '../../skills')</code> (<code>:57</code>)</li>
<li>Additive — never removes user paths</li>
<li>Relies on OpenCode Config singleton cache (<code>:101-102</code> comment)</li>
</ul>
<h3>2.2 Bootstrap module cache (<code>:49-96</code>)</h3>
<p><code>_bootstrapCache</code> (<code>:53</code>) — undefined=not loaded, null=missing file.</p>
<p><code>getBootstrapContent()</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li>Read <code>skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md</code> (<code>:67-71</code>)</li>
<li><code>extractAndStripFrontmatter</code> (<code>:16-34</code>) — simple line parser, no yaml dependency</li>
<li>Append OpenCode tool mapping (<code>:76-83</code>): TodoWrite→todowrite, Task→@mention subagents, Skill→native skill tool</li>
<li>Wrap in <code>&#x3C;EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT></code> (<code>:85-93</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>Performance: eliminates redundant fs+regex per agent step (#1202).</p>
<h3>2.3 Message transform (<code>:120-133</code>)</h3>
<p><code>experimental.chat.messages.transform</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Finds first user message (<code>:123-124</code>)</li>
<li>Skips if <code>EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT</code> already present (<code>:129</code>)</li>
<li>Unshifts bootstrap text before first part (<code>:131-132</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Rationale (<code>:111-114</code>): avoid system-message token bloat (#750) and Qwen multi-system breakage (#894).</p>
<h3>2.4 Path normalization (<code>:37-47</code>)</h3>
<p><code>normalizePath(p, homeDir)</code> — trim, <code>~/</code> expand, <code>path.resolve</code>.</p>
<p><code>OPENCODE_CONFIG_DIR</code> override (<code>:58-59</code>).</p>

</tbody>
</table>
<p>Uses <code>printf</code> not heredoc — bash 5.3+ hang (#571, <code>:44-45</code>).</p>
<h3>3.3 Content</h3>
<p>Full <code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md</code> embedded in session context (<code>:18</code>, <code>:35</code>) — differs from OpenCode which strips frontmatter.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Instruction Priority (behavioral config)</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/using-superpowers/SKILL.md:18-26</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li>User instructions (CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, AGENTS.md) — highest</li>
<li>Superpowers skills — override defaults</li>
<li>Default system prompt — lowest</li>
</ol>
<p>Skill-before-action rule (<code>:10-16</code>, <code>:46</code>): invoke skills before clarifying questions.</p>
<p>Platform adaptation (<code>:38-40</code>): non-CC hosts read <code>references/codex-tools.md</code>, <code>copilot-tools.md</code>, auto-loaded <code>gemini-tools.md</code>.</p>
<p>Red flags table (<code>:80-95</code>) — rationalization patterns that mean "stop and invoke skill".</p>
<p>Skill priority order (<code>:99-105</code>): process skills (brainstorming, debugging) before implementation skills.</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Sync Script Config Boundaries</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/scripts/sync-to-codex-plugin.sh:39-77</code> — <code>EXCLUDES</code> for Codex marketplace sync:</p>
<p>Anchored patterns (<code>:41-43</code>) prevent accidental exclusion of <code>skills/brainstorming/scripts/</code>.</p>
<p>Excluded host adapters: <code>.claude-plugin/</code>, <code>.cursor-plugin/</code>, <code>.opencode/</code>, <code>hooks/</code>, <code>GEMINI.md</code>, <code>gemini-extension.json</code>.</p>
<p>Destination: <code>prime-radiant-inc/openai-codex-plugins</code> fork, path <code>plugins/superpowers</code> (<code>:35-37</code>).</p>
<p>Bootstrap mode (<code>:23-25</code>, <code>:23</code>): <code>--bootstrap</code> creates plugin dir if missing.</p>

<h2>Appendix B — OpenCode <code>normalizePath</code> edge cases</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:37-47</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Empty string → <code>null</code> (<code>:39-40</code>)</li>
<li><code>~/foo</code> → <code>path.join(homeDir, 'foo')</code> (<code>:41-42</code>)</li>
<li><code>~</code> alone → <code>homeDir</code> (<code>:43-44</code>)</li>
<li>Otherwise <code>path.resolve(normalized)</code> (<code>:46</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p><code>OPENCODE_CONFIG_DIR</code> (<code>:58</code>) overrides default <code>~/.config/opencode</code> (<code>:59</code>).</p>

<h2>Appendix F — <code>using-superpowers</code> dot graph nodes (<code>SKILL.md:48-75</code>)</h2>
<p>The skill_flow digraph defines mandatory routing:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>User message received</code> → <code>Might any skill apply?</code></li>
<li>Yes → <code>Invoke Skill tool</code> → announce usage → checklist TodoWrite → follow skill</li>
<li><code>About to EnterPlanMode?</code> → brainstorm check branch</li>
<li>Red flag: skipping skill check before clarifying questions</li>
</ul>
<p>This graph is <strong>behavioral config</strong> embedded in skill text, not JSON.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 009_mcp-orchestration/09_sp_mcp.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers MCP Orchestration — Source Analysis</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code>. Superpowers는 <strong>MCP-native가 아니다</strong> — MCP server/client manager, <code>mcpServers</code> manifest, transport, OAuth, tool listing runtime을 구현하지 않는다. MCP는 skill <strong>작성 가이드</strong>와 <strong>호스트 MCP 도구 참조</strong>로만 등장한다.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2>2. Manifest Negative Evidence</h2>
<h3>2.1 Codex (<code>162_superpowers/.codex-plugin/plugin.json</code>)</h3>
<p>Keys present: <code>name</code>, <code>version</code>, <code>skills</code>, <code>interface</code> (<code>:1-47</code>).
Keys absent: <code>mcpServers</code>, <code>connectors</code>, <code>tools</code>, <code>permissions</code>.</p>
<h3>2.2 Claude (<code>162_superpowers/.claude-plugin/plugin.json:1-19</code>)</h3>
<p>Metadata only — no MCP declaration.</p>
<h3>2.3 Cursor (<code>162_superpowers/.cursor-plugin/plugin.json</code>)</h3>
<p>Declares <code>skills</code>, <code>agents</code>, <code>commands</code>, <code>hooks</code> — not MCP.</p>
<h3>2.4 Gemini (<code>162_superpowers/gemini-extension.json:1-6</code>)</h3>

<h3>2.5 OpenCode (<code>162_superpowers/.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js</code>)</h3>

<h2>3. MCP References Inside Skills (not implementation)</h2>
<h3>3.1 Skill authoring (<code>writing-skills/anthropic-best-practices.md:1053-1071</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-markdown">### MCP tool references
Format: ServerName:tool_name
Example: BigQuery:bigquery_schema, GitHub:create_issue
</code></pre>
<p>Purpose: avoid "tool not found" when <strong>host</strong> exposes multiple MCP servers.
SP does not implement BigQuery or GitHub servers — documents naming for skill authors.</p>
<h3>3.2 Copilot GitHub MCP (<code>copilot-tools.md:42</code>)</h3>
<p>Lists <code>github-mcp-server-*</code> as <strong>Copilot CLI native tools</strong> — issues, PRs, code search.
SP maps skill prose to host tools; does not bundle MCP server.</p>
<h3>3.3 brainstorming terminal state (<code>brainstorming/SKILL.md:66</code>)</h3>
<p>Explicit: after brainstorming invoke <strong>writing-plans only</strong> — NOT <code>mcp-builder</code> or implementation skills.</p>
<h3>3.4 TDD anti-pattern mock (<code>test-driven-development/testing-anti-patterns.md:144</code>)</h3>
<p><code>vi.mock('MCPServerManager')</code> — example in testing doc, not SP runtime.</p>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>Skill</code></td>
<td>native skill follow (<code>:12</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>Requires <code>[features] multi_agent = true</code> (<code>:18-24</code>).</p>
<p>Environment detection for worktrees (<code>:34-47</code>): <code>GIT_DIR</code>, <code>GIT_COMMON</code>, <code>BRANCH</code> bash probes.</p>
<p>Codex App finishing when sandbox blocks git (<code>:49-59</code>): commit + user uses App UI.</p>

<h3>4.4 OpenCode (<code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:76-83</code>)</h3>
<pre><code>TodoWrite → todowrite

<hr>
<h2>5. Subagent-Driven Development as Orchestration Layer</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:1-80</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fresh subagent per task (<code>:10-12</code>) — isolated context, no session pollution</li>
<li>Two-stage review: spec then quality (<code>:8</code>, <code>:54-59</code>)</li>
<li>Continuous execution — no human check-in between tasks (<code>:14</code>)</li>
<li>Process graph (<code>:18-33</code>) vs <code>executing-plans</code> for parallel session</li>
</ul>
<p>Prompt templates (separate files):</p>
<ul>
<li><code>implementer-prompt.md</code></li>
<li><code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code></li>
<li><code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Integration test (<code>docs/testing.md:40-64</code>) verifies Task tool dispatch via transcript JSONL.</p>
<h3>5.1 dispatching-parallel-agents</h3>
<p>Skill for independent parallel subagent tasks — maps to multiple <code>spawn_agent</code> / parallel <code>@generalist</code> per host mapping files.</p>
<h3>5.2 executing-plans</h3>
<p>Alternative when tasks need <strong>parallel session</strong> (worktree) vs same-session subagents.</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. OpenCode Plugin vs MCP</h2>
<p>OpenCode hosts may register MCP separately in user config. SP plugin only:</p>
<ol>
<li>Appends skills directory</li>
<li>Injects bootstrap on first user message</li>
</ol>
<p>No tool schema registration, no MCP <code>list_tools</code> bridge in SP code.</p>
<hr>

<h2>Appendix — Host orchestration decision tree</h2>

<th>Item</th>
<th>Detail</th>
</tr>

<td><code>dispatching-parallel-agents</code> — multiple host subagents</td>
</tr>

<pre><code class="language-bash">GIT_DIR=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)
GIT_COMMON=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-common-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)

<h2>코퍼스 — 010_memory-pipeline/10_sp_memory.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers Memory / Session Pipeline — Source Analysis</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code>. Superpowers는 <strong>learned-memory 엔진이 아니다</strong>. 기억은 procedural — reusable SKILL.md, session bootstrap, planning artifacts, subagent context discipline, optional brainstorm session files.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    SK["skills/*/SKILL.md&#x3C;br/>procedural memory"] --> AGENT["Agent behavior"]
    BOOT["SessionStart / OpenCode transform&#x3C;br/>session bootstrap"] --> AGENT
    SUB["subagent-driven-development&#x3C;br/>fresh context per task"] --> AGENT
    BRAIN[".superpowers/brainstorm/&#x3C;br/>visual companion artifacts"] --> SESSION["Project-local session files"]
    HOST["Host memory APIs&#x3C;br/>save_memory, store_memory"] --> LONG["Host long-term only"]
</code></pre>

<hr>
<h2>2. Procedural Memory — Skill Corpus</h2>
<p>14 first-party skills in <code>162_superpowers/skills/</code>:</p>
<p><code>brainstorming</code>, <code>dispatching-parallel-agents</code>, <code>executing-plans</code>, <code>finishing-a-development-branch</code>, <code>receiving-code-review</code>, <code>requesting-code-review</code>, <code>subagent-driven-development</code>, <code>systematic-debugging</code>, <code>test-driven-development</code>, <code>using-git-worktrees</code>, <code>using-superpowers</code>, <code>verification-before-completion</code>, <code>writing-plans</code>, <code>writing-skills</code>.</p>
<p>Each <code>SKILL.md</code> = durable <strong>how-to</strong> memory. No SP vector index — discovery via host skill loader + bootstrap text.</p>
<p><code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md:91-94</code> — "I remember this skill" red flag: skills evolve; must re-invoke.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. Session Bootstrap Pipeline</h2>
<h3>3.1 Claude/Cursor/Copilot SessionStart</h3>
<p><code>hooks/session-start:17-35</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Embeds full <code>using-superpowers/SKILL.md</code> in <code>session_context</code></li>
<li>Legacy path warning if <code>~/.config/superpowers/skills</code> exists (<code>:11-14</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p><code>hooks/hooks.json:5</code> — fires on <code>startup|clear|compact</code> — <strong>re-bootstrap after compact</strong>.</p>
<h3>3.2 OpenCode</h3>
<p><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:120-133</code> — bootstrap on first user message, not system.
Cache <code>_bootstrapCache</code> (<code>:53</code>) — survives per-step hook re-fire.</p>
<h3>3.3 Gemini</h3>
<p><code>GEMINI.md:1-2</code> — static context file imports bootstrap + tool mapping at session start.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Subagent Context Discipline (anti-memory-leak)</h2>
<p><code>subagent-driven-development/SKILL.md:10-12</code>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>They should never inherit your session's context or history — you construct exactly what they need.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Implications:</p>
<ul>
<li>No automatic transcript forwarding</li>
<li>Plan task text copied in full to subagent prompt (<code>:63</code> process — "extract all tasks with full text")</li>
<li>Preserves coordinator context for orchestration</li>
</ul>
<p><code>implementer-prompt.md</code>, <code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code>, <code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code> — curated review criteria as <strong>externalized memory</strong>.</p>
<p>Spec reviewer must read code independently (<code>docs/testing.md:51</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Brainstorm Visual Companion Session Files</h2>
<p><code>skills/brainstorming/visual-companion.md:29-48</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>screen_dir</code> — HTML content fragments</li>
<li><code>state_dir</code> — user selection events</li>
<li>Default persistence: <code>&#x3C;project>/.superpowers/brainstorm/&#x3C;session>/</code></li>
<li>Without <code>--project-dir</code>, <code>/tmp</code> cleanup (<code>:48</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Not long-term memory</strong> — design-session artifacts. User should <code>.gitignore</code> <code>.superpowers/</code> (<code>:48</code>).</p>
<p><code>server.cjs:76-79</code> — <code>BRAINSTORM_DIR</code>, <code>CONTENT_DIR</code> env configuration.</p>
<p>Server auto-exits after 30 min inactivity (<code>visual-companion.md:97</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>6. Verification Memory (completion gates)</h2>
<p><code>verification-before-completion/SKILL.md:18-38</code>:</p>
<pre><code>NO COMPLETION CLAIMS WITHOUT FRESH VERIFICATION EVIDENCE
</code></pre>
<p>Gate function: IDENTIFY command → RUN → READ output → VERIFY → claim (<code>:26-37</code>).</p>
<p>Does not persist results — requires <strong>fresh</strong> evidence each claim.</p>
<p>Common failures table (<code>:42-50</code>) — tests/linter/build/regression.</p>
<hr>

<hr>
<h2>8. Test Transcripts as External Memory</h2>
<p><code>docs/testing.md:1-64</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Integration tests run real Claude Code headless sessions</li>
<li>Verification parses <code>.jsonl</code> transcripts (<code>:57-63</code>)</li>
<li>Checks: Skill invocation, Task dispatch, TodoWrite, file creation, tests, git commits</li>
<li>Token analysis via <code>analyze-token-usage.py</code> (<code>:16</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Transcripts are <strong>host artifacts</strong> — SP reads for CI, does not own storage.</p>
<p>Requirements (<code>:36-38</code>): run from plugin directory, <code>claude</code> CLI, dev marketplace enabled.</p>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Context clear</td>
<td>SessionStart hook</td>
<td><code>hooks/hooks.json:5</code> matcher <code>clear</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Compact handoff</td>
<td>SessionStart hook</td>
<td><code>hooks/hooks.json:5</code> matcher <code>compact</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode first message</td>
<td>message transform</td>

<td>GEMINI.md import</td>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>After compact, SP re-injects full <code>using-superpowers</code> — <strong>session memory reset</strong> compensated by bootstrap, not by SP DB.</p>
<h2>Appendix B — <code>verification-before-completion</code> extended patterns</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/verification-before-completion/SKILL.md:76-140</code> region:</p>
<p>Test verification pattern (<code>:78-80</code> style): run command → cite output → claim.</p>
<p>Build verification: must see exit 0, not linter alone.</p>
<p>Agent completion: VCS diff required, not agent report.</p>
<p>Regression: red-green cycle required for new tests.</p>
<h2>Appendix C — Design doc artifact path</h2>
<p><code>brainstorming/SKILL.md:29</code>:</p>
<pre><code>docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-&#x3C;topic>-design.md
</code></pre>
<p>Committed to git — <strong>durable procedural artifact</strong>, not SP index.</p>
<p>Plans from <code>writing-plans</code> similarly produce plan documents reviewed before execution.</p>
<h2>Appendix D — <code>using-git-worktrees</code> memory of isolation</h2>
<p>Worktree skill Step 0 (<code>using-git-worktrees/SKILL.md</code>) — environment probes from <code>codex-tools.md:37-47</code>:</p>
<pre><code class="language-bash">GIT_DIR=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)
GIT_COMMON=$(cd "$(git rev-parse --git-common-dir)" 2>/dev/null &#x26;&#x26; pwd -P)
BRANCH=$(git branch --show-current)
</code></pre>
<p>Agent must <strong>re-read</strong> git state — no SP cache of worktree layout.</p>
<h2>Appendix E — Token analysis as session forensics</h2>
<p><code>docs/testing.md:64</code> — <code>analyze-token-usage.py</code> breaks down tokens by subagent from transcript.</p>
<p>Used for <strong>eval</strong>, not persistent memory — one-off analysis per test run.</p>
<h2>Appendix F — Copilot <code>store_memory</code> vs SP skills</h2>
<p><code>copilot-tools.md:38</code> — <code>store_memory</code> persists codebase facts for <strong>future Copilot sessions</strong>.</p>
<p>SP does not call or implement <code>store_memory</code> — skill text may mention memory concept; Copilot host executes.</p>
<p>Contrast: SP skills are <strong>git-versioned</strong> procedural memory always available when plugin installed.</p>
<h2>Appendix G — Brainstorm event file loop</h2>
<p><code>visual-companion.md:94-110</code> (loop section):</p>
<ol>
<li>Check <code>$STATE_DIR/server-info</code> alive</li>
<li>Write HTML to <code>screen_dir</code> with semantic filename</li>
<li>Read <code>state_dir/events</code> on next turn for user clicks</li>
<li>Never reuse filenames — each screen fresh file</li>
</ol>
<p>Event files = <strong>short-lived interaction memory</strong> between agent turns.</p>

<h2>Appendix — <code>executing-plans</code> vs session memory</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/executing-plans/SKILL.md</code> — parallel <strong>session</strong> execution in worktree. Memory model:</p>
<ul>
<li>Parent session retains plan context</li>
<li>Child session gets worktree-isolated copy — no automatic SP memory bridge</li>
<li>Plan text must be re-readable from committed plan file in worktree</li>
</ul>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/dispatching-parallel-agents/SKILL.md</code> — same-session parallel subagents share parent transcript but each subagent gets <strong>constructed</strong> prompt only.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>writing-plans</code> artifact discipline</h2>
<p>Plans must cite exact file paths and test commands — agents re-read plan file rather than SP memory index. Plan reviewer prompt (<code>writing-plans/plan-document-reviewer-prompt.md</code>) gates plan quality before execution begins.</p>
<h2>Appendix — OpenCode double-injection guard</h2>
<p><code>.opencode/plugins/superpowers.js:129</code> — if first user message already contains <code>EXTREMELY_IMPORTANT</code>, skip re-injection. Prevents bootstrap memory bloat when in-memory message arrays replay through hook on each agent step (<code>:116-118</code> comment).</p>

<h2>소스 코드 스니펫</h2>
<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TB
    SKILLS["skills/ (14 SKILL.md)"] --> CODEX[".codex-plugin/plugin.json"]
    SKILLS --> CLAUDE[".claude-plugin + hooks/"]

<hr>
<h2>2. Gate Detail with Source Lines</h2>
<h3>2.1 using-superpowers (<code>SKILL.md</code>)</h3>
<p>Instruction priority (<code>:18-26</code>): user > skills > default.</p>
<p>Red flags table (<code>:80-95</code>) — blocks rationalization ("simple question", "need context first").</p>
<p>Skill priority (<code>:99-105</code>): process skills before implementation skills.</p>
<p>SUBAGENT-STOP (<code>:6-8</code>): subagents skip bootstrap when dispatched for specific task.</p>
<h3>2.2 brainstorming HARD-GATE (<code>SKILL.md:12-14</code>)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-xml">&#x3C;HARD-GATE>
Do NOT invoke any implementation skill, write any code...
until design presented and user approved.
&#x3C;/HARD-GATE>
</code></pre>
<p>Checklist 9 steps (<code>:22-32</code>) — each as TodoWrite task.</p>
<p>Terminal state (<code>:66</code>): <strong>only</strong> <code>writing-plans</code> after brainstorming — not mcp-builder.</p>
<p>Design doc path (<code>:29</code>): <code>docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-&#x3C;topic>-design.md</code>.</p>
<h3>2.3 test-driven-development (<code>SKILL.md:31-45</code>)</h3>
<p>Iron law:</p>
<pre><code>NO PRODUCTION CODE WITHOUT A FAILING TEST FIRST
</code></pre>
<p>Write code before test? Delete and restart (<code>:37-45</code>). No exceptions.</p>
<p>Red-Green-Refactor graph (<code>:49-60</code>). Exceptions only with human partner (<code>:24-28</code>).</p>
<h3>2.4 subagent-driven-development (<code>SKILL.md:8-80</code>)</h3>
<p>Two-stage review per task:</p>
<ol>
<li>Spec compliance reviewer (<code>spec-reviewer-prompt.md</code>)</li>
<li>Code quality reviewer (<code>code-quality-reviewer-prompt.md</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>Loop on failure — re-dispatch implementer (<code>:75-80</code>).</p>
<p>Continuous execution (<code>:14</code>): no "should I continue?" between tasks.</p>
<p>Final code reviewer + <code>finishing-a-development-branch</code> (<code>:66</code> graph).</p>
<h3>2.5 verification-before-completion (<code>SKILL.md:18-74</code>)</h3>
<p>Iron law (<code>:18-22</code>):</p>
<pre><code>NO COMPLETION CLAIMS WITHOUT FRESH VERIFICATION EVIDENCE
</code></pre>
<p>Gate function 5 steps (<code>:26-37</code>). Rationalization table (<code>:65-74</code>).</p>
<p>Claims vs evidence table (<code>:42-50</code>).</p>
<h3>2.6 requesting-code-review</h3>
<p><code>code-reviewer.md</code> — severity tiers; critical/important findings <strong>block</strong> merge.</p>
<p>Skill triggered before PR / after major changes.</p>
<h3>2.7 finishing-a-development-branch</h3>
<p>Tests must pass before branch finish options presented to human.
Discard requires explicit confirmation — destructive gate.</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. What SP Does NOT Guard</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Concern</th>
<th>Owner</th>
<th>SP role</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Shell command approval</td>
<td>host (Codex sandbox, Claude permissions)</td>
<td>none</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCP tool allow/deny</td>
<td>host MCP config</td>
<td>documents MCP naming only</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network/file sandbox</td>
<td>host</td>
<td><code>codex-tools.md</code> App handoff when blocked</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secret leakage</td>
<td>host + user</td>
<td>no SP scanner</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dangerous tool calls</td>
<td>host PreToolUse hooks</td>
<td>SP hooks lack PreToolUse</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>SP guards <strong>wrong work, skipped tests, unreviewed code, false completion</strong> — not security perimeter.</p>

<h2>Appendix B — TDD red flags (<code>test-driven-development/SKILL.md:60-120</code> region)</h2>
<p>Rationalization table — "skip TDD just this once", "throwaway" without human OK, "config files exception" without ask.</p>
<p>Deletion rule (<code>:37-45</code>) — code written before test must be deleted entirely.</p>
<h2>Appendix C — <code>requesting-code-review</code> severity model</h2>
<p><code>code-reviewer.md</code> in <code>skills/requesting-code-review/</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Critical findings → must fix before proceed</li>
<li>Important findings → must fix or explicit waive</li>
<li>Minor → optional</li>
</ul>
<p>Pairs with <code>receiving-code-review</code> for agent discipline when feedback arrives.</p>
<h2>Appendix D — <code>finishing-a-development-branch</code> human gates</h2>
<p>Skill requires:</p>
<ul>
<li>Tests pass first</li>
<li>Structured options: merge, PR, discard</li>
<li>Discard requires explicit human confirmation — <strong>destructive approval</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>When Codex sandbox blocks git (<code>codex-tools.md:49-59</code>), agent commits and defers branch/PR to App UI — host guardian replaces git skill gates.</p>
<h2>Appendix E — <code>systematic-debugging</code> as pre-fix guardian</h2>
<p>Forces root-cause before patch — prevents "try random fix" loop.</p>
<p>Integrates with TDD: failing test proves fix, verification-before-completion proves claim.</p>
<h2>Appendix F — Hook absence = no tool guardian</h2>
<p>Complete hook registration in SP:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">// hooks/hooks.json — ONLY SessionStart
"SessionStart": [...]
</code></pre>
<p>No <code>PreToolUse</code>, <code>PostToolUse</code>, <code>PermissionRequest</code> — compare Claude Code host hooks for tool approval.</p>
<h2>Appendix G — SDD integration test assertion list</h2>
<p>From <code>docs/testing.md:44-51</code>:</p>
<ol>
<li>Plan loaded once at start</li>
<li>Full task text to subagents</li>
<li>Self-review before report</li>
<li>Spec review before quality review</li>
<li>Review loops on failure</li>
<li>Spec reviewer reads code independently</li>
</ol>
<p>Each assertion = <strong>guardian behavior</strong> verified via transcript, not compile-time check.</p>

<h2>Appendix — <code>requesting-code-review</code> workflow</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/requesting-code-review/SKILL.md</code> — dispatch review before merge. <code>code-reviewer.md</code> template defines:</p>
<ul>
<li>Severity tiers (critical / important / minor)</li>
<li>Blocking behavior on critical and important</li>
<li>Expected output format for reviewer agent</li>
</ul>
<p>Pairs with integration test <code>tests/claude-code/test-requesting-code-review.sh</code>.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>receiving-code-review</code> anti-rationalization</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/receiving-code-review/SKILL.md</code> — when feedback arrives, agent must not argue or explain away findings. Guardian against <strong>ego-driven</strong> dismissal of review — complements outbound review skill.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>systematic-debugging</code> phases</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/skills/systematic-debugging/SKILL.md</code> — five-phase methodology before fix:</p>
<ol>
<li>Reproduce reliably</li>
<li>Understand scope</li>
<li>Form hypothesis</li>
<li>Test hypothesis minimally</li>
<li>Fix with regression test (links to TDD iron law)</li>
</ol>
<p>Prevents "shotgun debugging" — process guardian for bug work.</p>
<h2>Appendix — Contributor PR guardian (<code>AGENTS.md:52-54</code>)</h2>
<p>Speculative fixes rejected — every PR must solve a problem someone <strong>actually experienced</strong>. Session transcript or error required. This is <strong>human-process guardian</strong> for repo quality, parallel to agent skill gates.</p>

<h2>3. Visual Companion (NOT web search)</h2>

<li>Platform launch notes: Claude Windows <code>run_in_background</code> (<code>:58-64</code>), Codex <code>CODEX_CI</code> (<code>:67-72</code>), Gemini <code>--foreground</code> (<code>:74-79</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p><code>server.cjs:1-80</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>WebSocket RFC6455 implementation (<code>:6-72</code>)</li>
<li>Random port <code>49152 + random</code> (<code>:76</code>)</li>
<li>Default host <code>127.0.0.1</code> (<code>:77</code>)</li>
<li>Session dir from <code>BRAINSTORM_DIR</code> env (<code>:79</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Classification</strong>: local HTTP display + click events — <strong>not</strong> internet search/crawl.</p>
<p>Tests: <code>tests/brainstorm-server/server.test.js</code>, <code>ws-protocol.test.js</code>.</p>

<h2>6. Contributor Governance (<code>AGENTS.md</code>)</h2>
<p>Key rules for agents (<code>:11-20</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Complete PR template</li>
<li>Search open+closed PRs</li>
<li>Verify real problem</li>
<li>Core vs standalone plugin</li>
<li>Disclose model/harness/plugins</li>
<li>Human approves full diff</li>
</ol>
<p>Will not accept (<code>:34-59</code>):</p>
<ul>
<li>Third-party dependencies (except new harness)</li>
<li>"Compliance" skill rewrites without eval evidence</li>
<li>Project-specific config in core</li>
<li>Bulk spray-and-pray PRs</li>
<li>Speculative fixes</li>
<li>Domain-specific skills in core</li>
</ul>
<p>Target branch: <code>dev</code> not <code>main</code> (<code>:32</code>).</p>

<h2>Appendix A — README workflow philosophy (<code>README.md:9-19</code>)</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/README.md:11-17</code> core loop:</p>
<ol>
<li>Agent asks what user is really trying to do — not immediate code</li>
<li>Spec teased in digestible chunks</li>
<li>Implementation plan for "junior engineer with poor taste" — TDD, YAGNI, DRY</li>
<li>Subagent-driven-development — autonomous hours-long execution</li>
</ol>
<p>"Skills trigger automatically" (<code>:19</code>) — bootstrap + host skill loader, not SP daemon.</p>

<h2>Appendix — <code>README.md</code> install harness list (cross-cutting)</h2>
<p><code>162_superpowers/README.md:7</code> — Quickstart links: Claude Code, Codex CLI, Codex App, Factory Droid, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Cursor, GitHub Copilot CLI.</p>
<p>Each harness section below documents install commands — no unified SP daemon installer.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>tests/explicit-skill-requests/</code> harness</h2>
<p><code>run-test.sh</code>, <code>run-multiturn-test.sh</code>, <code>run-claude-describes-sdd.sh</code> — verify agents invoke skills when user explicitly requests skill behavior across turns.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>tests/codex-plugin-sync/</code></h2>
<p><code>test-sync-to-codex-plugin.sh</code> — deterministic sync verification; same SHA → identical PR diff (<code>sync-to-codex-plugin.sh:12-13</code>).</p>
<h2>Appendix — Brainstorm <code>start-server.sh</code> lifecycle</h2>
<p><code>skills/brainstorming/scripts/start-server.sh</code> — launches <code>server.cjs</code>, writes <code>server-info</code> JSON to state dir, supports <code>--foreground</code>, <code>--project-dir</code>, <code>--host</code>, <code>--url-host</code> flags referenced in <code>visual-companion.md:36-90</code>.</p>
<p><code>stop-server.sh</code> — clean shutdown; creates <code>server-stopped</code> marker read by visual-companion loop.</p>
<h2>Appendix — <code>.opencode/INSTALL.md</code> cross-ref</h2>
<p>OpenCode install path separate from Codex marketplace — documents copying plugin or marketplace entry for OpenCode.ai users. Part of multi-harness distribution story (<code>README.md:33</code>).</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 014_web-search/14_sp_web-search.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Superpowers Web/Search — Source Analysis</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>162_superpowers/</code>. Superpowers는 <strong>독립 web-search 엔진을 구현하지 않는다</strong> — crawler, browser automation runtime, search API wrapper, MCP web-search provider 없음. Search는 <strong>호스트 tool</strong>이거나 <strong>없음</strong>. Web-adjacent surface는 (1) host tool mapping docs, (2) brainstorming <strong>local HTML server</strong> — 둘 다 internet search 아님.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph LR
    SP["Superpowers skills"] --> MAP["references/*-tools.md&#x3C;br/>host tool names"]

    HOST --> WS["google_web_search / web_fetch&#x3C;br/>(if host provides)"]
    SP --> VC["brainstorming visual-companion&#x3C;br/>localhost HTTP server"]
    VC --> LOCAL[".superpowers/brainstorm/&#x3C;br/>NOT internet"]

<h2>2. Host Tool Mapping Files (skills/using-superpowers/references/)</h2>
<p>SP documents <strong>how skills should call host tools</strong> — not executes search itself.</p>
<h3>2.1 Codex (<code>codex-tools.md:1-60</code>)</h3>
<p>Maps: Task→spawn_agent, TodoWrite→update_plan, Read/Write/Bash→native.</p>
<p><strong>No WebSearch or WebFetch row</strong> in mapping table (<code>:5-14</code>) — Codex search is host config concern, not SP skill mapping.</p>
<p>Documents <code>multi_agent</code> feature flag (<code>:18-24</code>) and git environment probes (<code>:34-47</code>).</p>
<h3>2.2 Gemini (<code>gemini-tools.md:5-17</code>)</h3>

<h2>3. Skills Mentioning Search (prose only)</h2>
<p>Skills may say "search official docs" in methodology text — <strong>host executes</strong> if configured.</p>
<p><code>writing-skills/anthropic-best-practices.md</code> — progressive disclosure, not search runtime.</p>
<p><code>systematic-debugging</code> — may recommend repro steps; no bundled search tool.</p>
<p><strong>Parity</strong>: compare <code>014_web-search/14_co_web-search.md</code> for Codex <code>web_search</code> builtin in <code>codex-rs</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Visual Companion — Local HTML Server (NOT web search)</h2>
<h3>4.1 Purpose (<code>visual-companion.md:1-25</code>)</h3>
<p>Browser-based <strong>local</strong> companion for mockups, diagrams, layout comparisons.</p>
<p>Decision rule (<code>:7-8</code>): "would user understand better by seeing than reading?"</p>
<p>Terminal for text/tabular questions (<code>:17-24</code>) — even UI topics can be conceptual.</p>
<h3>4.2 Architecture (<code>visual-companion.md:27-48</code>)</h3>
<ul>
<li>Server watches directory for HTML files</li>
<li>Serves newest to browser</li>
<li>User clicks → events to <code>state_dir/events</code></li>
<li>Persistence: <code>--project-dir</code> → <code>.superpowers/brainstorm/</code> (<code>:46-48</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p>Startup JSON (<code>:39-41</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{"type":"server-started","port":52341,"url":"http://localhost:52341",
 "screen_dir":".../content","state_dir":".../state"}
</code></pre>
<h3>4.3 server.cjs (<code>skills/brainstorming/scripts/server.cjs</code>)</h3>

<li>SP never spawns search on behalf of agent</li>

<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>
<h2>Installed CLI version pin (2026-06-27)</h2>
<p>Single source of truth for pinned <code>ay</code>/<code>cr</code>/<code>gr</code>/<code>ki</code> binaries:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>015_reverse-engineering/36_installed_cli_version_manifest.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>WP5 trace shards (<code>38</code>–<code>41</code>) extend hubs without changing evidence-level definitions above.</p>

<p>2026-06-27 pass — installed CLI practical RE (goal <code>4e94e12d-a9b</code>):</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/23_grok_inspect_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>Grok Inspect Trace</h1>
<p>This pass used disposable temp <code>HOME</code> and workspace directories. It did not run model prompts, authenticate, read private Grok sessions, or mutate the user's real Grok config.</p>

<p>Command:</p>
<ul>

<p>Help says this command shows the configuration Grok discovers for the current directory and can emit machine-readable JSON.</p>

<h2>Documentation Consequences</h2>
<ul>
<li>Grok agent discovery is no longer only bundled-doc and binary-string evidence. Public <code>inspect --json</code> exposes discovered user/project agents and skills without a model session.</li>
<li><code>inspect --json</code> is a useful no-model verification path for future plugin, permission, MCP, LSP, and marketplace traces.</li>
<li>Agent definitions in this trace use Markdown frontmatter. Inline <code>--agents &#x3C;JSON></code> still remains a separate execution-time path and was not schema-validated here.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Remaining Gaps</h2>
<ul>
<li>Inline <code>--agents &#x3C;JSON></code> schema and execution semantics.</li>
<li>Plugin-provided agent/skill discovery through <code>inspect --json</code> is traced in <code>015_reverse-engineering/28_grok_plugin_inspect_trace.md</code>.</li>
<li>MCP/LSP discovery from synthetic config through <code>inspect --json</code>.</li>
<li>Permission source precedence.</li>
<li>Actual child-session scheduling and isolation behavior during model execution.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/28_grok_plugin_inspect_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>Grok Plugin Inspect Trace</h1>
<p>This pass used disposable temp <code>HOME</code>, workspace, and local plugin directories. It did not install into the user's real Grok config, run model prompts, authenticate, call remote marketplaces, or read private sessions.</p>
<h2>Synthetic Plugin</h2>
<p>The temp plugin contained:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>plugin.json</code> with <code>name</code>, <code>version</code>, and <code>description</code></li>
<li><code>skills/trace/SKILL.md</code></li>
<li><code>agents/trace.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>The plugin was installed with:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>HOME=&#x3C;tmp>/home ~/.local/bin/grok plugin install &#x3C;tmp>/plugin --trust</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Then discovery state was read with:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>HOME=&#x3C;tmp>/home ~/.local/bin/grok --cwd &#x3C;tmp>/ws inspect --json</code></li>
</ul>

<p>Implication: plugin-provided agents are namespaced with <code>&#x3C;plugin-name>:&#x3C;agent-name></code> in the inspect output, while plugin-provided skills keep their skill name and carry plugin metadata in <code>source</code>.</p>
<h2>Documentation Consequences</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>grok inspect --json</code> is a verified no-model path for installed plugin discovery.</li>
<li>Trusted local plugin install does not merely copy files; it affects runtime discovery for plugin-provided skills and agents.</li>
<li>This trace used only skills and agents. Hook, MCP, and LSP execution/loading remain separate traces because those can launch code or processes.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Remaining Gaps</h2>
<ul>
<li>Inspect output for plugin-provided hooks, MCP servers, and LSP servers after trusted install.</li>
<li>Disable/enable effects on <code>inspect --json</code>.</li>
<li>Marketplace plugin discovery and namespacing.</li>
<li>Actual plugin agent execution semantics.</li>
</ul>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/45_ki_codewhisperer_wire_stream_oauth.md</code></h3>
<h1>45 — ki: CodeWhisperer wire + stream + OAuth contract (LIVE-confirmed)</h1>
<blockquote>
<p>상태: ✅ 라이브 확정 (2026-06-28). jawcode <code>packages/ai/src/providers/kiro.ts</code>
실측 + <code>JWC_KIRO_DEBUG</code> 라이브 캡처(<code>jwc -p --model kiro/claude-sonnet-4.5</code>) + kiro2api
<code>types/codewhisperer.go@859a47c9</code> 교차검증.
보완 대상: <code>15_ki_reverse.md</code>(Rust 내부), <code>43_ki_auth_session_boundary_trace.md</code>(auth).
이 문서는 Kiro CLI <strong>내부</strong>가 아니라, 서드파티 하니스가 Kiro 백엔드를 직접 호출할 때의
<strong>CodeWhisperer 와이어 프로토콜</strong>을 다룬다 (opencodex/jawcode kiro provider 기준).</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>0. 엔드포인트 / 헤더</h2>
<pre><code>POST https://runtime.{region}.kiro.dev/            (기본 region us-east-1)
authorization: Bearer {accessToken}
content-type:  application/x-amz-json-1.0
accept:        application/vnd.amazon.eventstream
x-amz-target:  AmazonCodeWhispererStreamingService.GenerateAssistantResponse
user-agent:    aws-sdk-js/1.0.27 ua/2.1 os/{os} lang/js md/nodejs#22.x
               api/codewhispererstreaming#1.0.27 m/E KiroIDE-{ver}-{fingerprint}
x-amz-user-agent:            aws-sdk-js/1.0.27 KiroIDE-{ver}-{fingerprint}
x-amzn-codewhisperer-optout: true
x-amzn-kiro-agent-mode:      vibe
x-amzn-kiro-profile-arn:     {profileArn}        (바이너리 분석에서 발견된 전용 헤더)
amz-sdk-invocation-id:       {uuid}              (매 요청 새로)
</code></pre>
<p>SigV4 불필요 — Bearer 전용. 응답은 <code>application/vnd.amazon.eventstream</code> 바이너리 프레이밍.</p>
<h2>1. 요청 바디 — conversationState (와이어 계약 3대 규칙, 실측 확정)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "conversationState": {
    "chatTriggerType": "MANUAL",
    "conversationId": "&#x3C;stable 16-hex>",
    "currentMessage": { "userInputMessage": {
      "content": "&#x3C;non-empty>", "modelId": "&#x3C;id>", "origin": "AI_EDITOR",
      "userInputMessageContext": { "tools": [...], "toolResults": [...] }
    }},
    "history": [ {"userInputMessage": {...}}, {"assistantResponseMessage": {...}}, ... ]
  },
  "profileArn": "&#x3C;arn>"
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>규칙 1 — history 엄격 교대.</strong> <code>history</code>는 user/assistant 턴이 반드시 교대해야 한다.
연속 user/assistant는 거부.</p>
<p><strong>규칙 2 — toolResult 인접.</strong> 각 <code>toolResult</code>는, 그 결과를 낸 <code>assistantResponseMessage</code>
(=<code>toolUses</code> 보유) <strong>바로 다음</strong> <code>userInputMessage</code>의 <code>userInputMessageContext.toolResults</code>에
실려야 한다. 모든 toolResult를 마지막 메시지에 몰아넣으면(평탄 누적) →
<code>REQUEST_BODY_INVALID / "Improperly formed request"</code> (400).</p>
<p><strong>규칙 3 — toolUses[].input 은 JSON 객체.</strong> (kiro2api <code>ToolUseEntry.Input map[string]any</code>)</p>
<pre><code class="language-jsonc">// 올바름                              // 틀림 → 400
{ "toolUseId": "...", "name": "bash",  { ..., "input": "{\"command\":\"echo\"}" }  // 문자열 금지
  "input": { "command": "echo" } }
</code></pre>
<p><code>JSON.stringify(args)</code>로 보내면 tool 호출이 포함된 <strong>모든</strong> 요청이 400. (과거 no-tool 채팅만
통과해서 이 결함이 오래 숨어 있었음.)</p>
<p>추가 계약:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>toolResults[].content</code> = <code>[{ "text": "..." }]</code> 배열, <code>status</code> = <code>"success"|"error"</code>,
<code>toolUseId</code> (양쪽 정규화 <code>^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{1,64}$</code>로 일치시킬 것).</li>
<li><code>userInputMessage.content</code>는 비어 있으면 안 됨 → tool 결과만 보낼 땐 placeholder(<code>"(tool results)"</code>).</li>
<li><code>origin: "AI_EDITOR"</code>, <code>chatTriggerType: "MANUAL"</code>.</li>
<li>(kiro2api에는 <code>agentTaskType:"vibe"</code>, <code>agentContinuationId</code>, <code>images[]</code> 필드도 있으나
no-tool/tool 경로 모두 생략해도 통과 — optional.)</li>
</ul>
<h2>2. 스트리밍 응답 — tool 이벤트 프로토콜 (라이브 캡처로 확정)</h2>
<p>AWS eventstream 프레임의 각 event payload는 JSON. <strong>CodeWhisperer는 tool 이벤트마다
<code>name</code>+<code>toolUseId</code>를 반복 포함한다</strong> (이게 파싱의 함정):</p>
<pre><code>{"name":"bash","toolUseId":"tooluse_X"}                    # start (input 없음)
{"input":"","name":"bash","toolUseId":"tooluse_X"}         # input 조각 (name 포함!)
{"input":"{\"command\": \"ec","name":"bash","toolUseId":"tooluse_X"}
{"input":"ho hi\"}","name":"bash","toolUseId":"tooluse_X"} # 조각들 이어붙이면 완전한 JSON
{"name":"bash","stop":true,"toolUseId":"tooluse_X"}        # stop (name 포함)
</code></pre>
<ul>
<li>일반 텍스트: <code>{"content":"..."}</code></li>
<li>토큰 사용량: <code>{"usage":N}</code></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>파싱 규칙: <code>name</code> 유무로 판별하지 말 것.</strong> 반드시 <code>stop===true</code> → <code>"input" in payload</code>
→ <code>name</code> 순으로 판별. (<code>name</code>만 보면 모든 input 조각이 새 tool_start로 오인돼 인자가 빈
<code>{}</code>가 됨 → tool이 "expected string, received undefined"로 실패.) <code>input</code> 조각을 toolUseId별로
이어붙여 stop에서 <code>JSON.parse</code>.</p>
<p>병렬 다중 tool: 관측상 <strong>순차</strong> 스트리밍(toolUse A start→조각→stop, 그다음 B). 단일
<code>currentToolCall</code> 누적으로 충분하나, 견고성을 위해 toolUseId 매칭/lazy-start 권장.</p>
<h2>3. OAuth / 토큰</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>경로</th>
<th>위치 / 방법</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>kiro-cli SQLite</td>
<td><code>~/Library/Application Support/kiro-cli/data.sqlite3</code>, <code>~/.kiro/sso/cache.db</code> — <code>auth_kv</code> 테이블, key <code>kirocli:social:token</code>/<code>kirocli:odic:token</code>/<code>codewhisperer:odic:token</code>, value JSON <code>{access_token, refresh_token, profile_arn, expires_at, region}</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Kiro Desktop refresh</td>
<td><code>POST https://prod.{region}.auth.desktop.kiro.dev/refreshToken</code> body <code>{refreshToken}</code> → <code>{accessToken, refreshToken, expiresIn}</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AWS SSO OIDC refresh</td>
<td><code>POST https://oidc.{region}.amazonaws.com/token</code> (grantType refresh_token)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>prokiro 프록시</td>
<td><code>~/.prokiro/auth.json</code> <code>{accessToken, refreshToken, profileArn, region, expiresAt}</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>토큰 형식</td>
<td>accessToken 접두사 <code>aoa</code> (가비지 credential 방어용 검증)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>401 처리</td>
<td>refresh 후 1회 재시도, 실패 시 캐시 무효화</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>만료</td>
<td>60초 전 사전 refresh</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<blockquote>
<p>참고 버그: kiro-cli가 갱신 토큰을 SQLite에 다시 안 쓰는 케이스 보고 → 외부 임포트 시 갱신 충돌 주의
(kirodotdev/Kiro#4847).</p>
</blockquote>
<h2>4. 모델 id (kiro provider, jawcode)</h2>
<p><code>claude-opus-4.8/4.7/4.6/4.5</code>, <code>claude-sonnet-4.6/4.5/4</code>, <code>claude-haiku-4.5</code>,
<code>deepseek-3.2</code>, <code>minimax-m2.5/m2.1</code>, <code>glm-5</code>, <code>qwen3-coder-next</code> → provider <code>kiro</code>,
api <code>kiro-streaming</code>. (provider/model 형식: <code>kiro/claude-sonnet-4.5</code>.)</p>
<h2>5. ToS 주의</h2>
<p>Kiro 공식 FAQ가 서드파티 하니스 사용을 명시 금지. 403 <code>TEMPORARILY_SUSPENDED</code>,
<code>AccountSuspendedException</code>, 423 Locked 등 계정 정지 보고 다수. 개인 실험 한정.</p>

<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>

<td>Codex</td>
<td>Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</td>
<td>엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</td>
<td>가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</td>
<td>보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</td>

</tr>

<td>Aider</td>

<td>RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-commit, 최소 마찰 CLI 경험.</td>
<td>개인 개발자, 빠른 코드 편집, 낮은 학습 비용이 중요한 사용 사례</td>
<td>[[00_ai_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td>TypeScript + React/Ink + Zod + A2A server + multi-package monorepo</td>
<td>schema-first와 policy-first를 결합해 CLI를 확장 운영체계처럼 다룬다.</td>
<td>PromptProvider/Scheduler/PolicyEngine/ModelRouter/ExtensionManager가 분리된 가장 운영형 TypeScript engine.</td>
<td>엔터프라이즈 CLI, 확장 운영, 정책 감사, TypeScript 기반 재구현</td>
<td>[[00_ge_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode</td>
<td>TypeScript + Bun + Effect-TS + Hono + SolidJS + Tauri</td>
<td>agent runtime을 웹/데스크톱/SDK가 공유하는 product platform으로 본다.</td>
<td>Effect-TS service layer, 21+ provider, plugin SDK, session replay, multi-surface delivery.</td>
<td>빠른 제품화, GUI/desktop 포함, TS로 직접 확장하고 싶은 팀</td>
<td>[[00_oc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td>TypeScript/JavaScript bundle + React/Ink + custom renderer + Anthropic runtime</td>
<td>제품 사용성을 최우선으로 하면서 hook, security chain, memory, MCP를 깊게 묶는다.</td>
<td>가장 풍부한 productized tool surface, deepest shell security, strongest file-based memory UX.</td>
<td>상용 CLI UX, 강한 shell security, memory-heavy workflows, enterprise policy integration</td>
<td>[[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]]</td>
</tr>

<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>Aider</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-com</li>
</ul>
